:root{
  /* Motion tokens — exponential decel curves, not bounces */
  --ease-out-quart:cubic-bezier(.25,1,.5,1);
  --ease-out-expo:cubic-bezier(.19,1,.22,1);
  --ease-out-smooth:cubic-bezier(.2,0,0,1);
  --ease-standard:cubic-bezier(.4,0,.2,1);
  --ease-spring:cubic-bezier(.34,1.2,.64,1);

  --dur-instant:120ms;
  --dur-fast:180ms;
  --dur-normal:280ms;
  --dur-slow:420ms;
  --dur-hero:620ms;

  --display-font:'Chakra Petch','Orbitron',sans-serif;
  --hero-font:'Unbounded','Orbitron',sans-serif;
  --body-font:'Manrope','Inter',sans-serif;
  --mono-font:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;
}

<script>
// ═══════════ TELEGRAM + STORAGE ═══════════
// Telegram WebApp handle (may be undefined in regular browser)
const TG = window.Telegram && window.Telegram.WebApp ? window.Telegram.WebApp : null;

// Current authenticated user profile
let USER = null;                 // {id, first_name, last_name, username, photo_url, language_code}
let USE_CLOUD = false;           // true when Telegram CloudStorage is available
let SYNC_STATUS = 'pending';     // 'pending' | 'ok' | 'local' | 'error'

// Known storage keys (loaded in bulk on init)
const KNOWN_KEYS = ['smc_pts','smc_journal','smc_sim_best','smc_done','smc_quiz_done','smc_registered','smc_registered_at','smc_profile'];

// In-memory cache — allows SYNC read while Cloud is async
const CACHE = {};

// Build storage key scoped to current user (so multiple users on same browser
// don't overwrite each other in localStorage).
function userKey(k){
  const uid = USER && USER.id ? USER.id : 'guest';
  return 'u' + uid + ':' + k;
}

// --- SYNC read (from in-memory cache, fallback to localStorage) ---
function ls(k, def=null){
  if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(CACHE, k)) {
    return CACHE[k] === null || CACHE[k] === undefined ? def : CACHE[k];
  }
  try {
    const v = localStorage.getItem(userKey(k));
    if (v === null) return def;
    const parsed = JSON.parse(v);
    CACHE[k] = parsed;
    return parsed;
  } catch { return def; }
}

// --- Write-through save: cache → localStorage → CloudStorage (async) ---
function lsSave(k, v){
  CACHE[k] = v;
  try { localStorage.setItem(userKey(k), JSON.stringify(v)); } catch {}
  if (USE_CLOUD) {
    try {
      TG.CloudStorage.setItem(k, JSON.stringify(v), (err) => {
        if (err) { SYNC_STATUS = 'error'; }
      });
    } catch {}
  }
}

// Bulk-load all known keys from CloudStorage into CACHE.
// Falls back to localStorage (per-user scoped) if Cloud is unavailable or empty.
function loadUserData(){
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    // 0. One-time migration: old builds stored keys without user prefix.
    //    Copy them into the current user's scope so progress is preserved.
    KNOWN_KEYS.forEach(k => {
      try {
        const scoped = userKey(k);
        if (localStorage.getItem(scoped) === null) {
          const legacy = localStorage.getItem(k);
          if (legacy !== null) localStorage.setItem(scoped, legacy);
        }
      } catch {}
    });

    // 1. Seed cache from localStorage — immediate, works offline
    KNOWN_KEYS.forEach(k => {
      try {
        const v = localStorage.getItem(userKey(k));
        if (v !== null) CACHE[k] = JSON.parse(v);
      } catch {}
    });

    if (!USE_CLOUD) { SYNC_STATUS = 'local'; resolve(); return; }

    // Merge: CloudStorage wins when its value is present (truth source across devices)
    try {
      TG.CloudStorage.getItems(KNOWN_KEYS, (err, result) => {
        if (err) { SYNC_STATUS = 'error'; resolve(); return; }
        let merged = 0;
        KNOWN_KEYS.forEach(k => {
          const raw = result && result[k];
          if (raw !== undefined && raw !== null && raw !== '') {
            try {
              const val = JSON.parse(raw);
              CACHE[k] = val;
              localStorage.setItem(userKey(k), raw); // keep local in sync
              merged++;
            } catch {}
          }
        });
        SYNC_STATUS = 'ok';
        resolve();
      });
    } catch { SYNC_STATUS = 'error'; resolve(); }
  });
}

// Force re-pull from cloud (user-triggered)
async function syncNow(){
  if (!USE_CLOUD) { showToast('☁️ CloudStorage недоступний'); return; }
  showToast('🔄 Синхронізація…');
  await loadUserData();
  updPtsDisplay();
  if (typeof renderHome === 'function' && cur === 'home') renderHome();
  updateProfileSheet();
  showToast('✅ Синхронізовано');
}

// Wipe all progress for current user (local + cloud)
function confirmReset(){
  if (!confirm('Скинути весь прогрес? Балів, пройдені модулі та журнал буде видалено.')) return;
  KNOWN_KEYS.forEach(k => {
    delete CACHE[k];
    try { localStorage.removeItem(userKey(k)); } catch {}
    if (USE_CLOUD) { try { TG.CloudStorage.removeItem(k, ()=>{}); } catch {} }
  });
  done = new Set();
  quizDone = new Set();
  updPtsDisplay();
  closeProfile();
  goHome();
  showToast('🗑 Прогрес очищено');
}

// ═══════════ POINTS ═══════════
function getPoints(){return ls('smc_pts',0);}
function addPoints(n){const p=getPoints()+n;lsSave('smc_pts',p);updPtsDisplay();showToast('⭐ +'+n+' балів!');}
function updPtsDisplay(){const p=getPoints();document.querySelectorAll('.pts-num').forEach(el=>el.textContent=p);}

// ═══════════ TOAST ═══════════
let toastTimer;
function showToast(msg){const t=document.getElementById('toast');t.textContent=msg;t.classList.add('show');clearTimeout(toastTimer);toastTimer=setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove('show'),2200);}

// ═══════════ NAV ═══════════
let cur='title', hist=[], curPath='all';
function showS(id){
  document.querySelectorAll('.screen').forEach(s=>s.classList.remove('active'));
  const el=document.getElementById('s-'+id);
  if(el) el.classList.add('active');
  cur=id;
  const isTitle=id==='title';
  document.getElementById('bnav').style.display=isTitle?'none':'flex';
  ['menu','paths','tools','gloss'].forEach(n=>document.getElementById('bn-'+n)?.classList.remove('active'));
  if(id==='home')document.getElementById('bn-menu')?.classList.add('active');
  if(id==='menu')document.getElementById('bn-paths')?.classList.add('active');
  if(['tools','calc','journal','simulator'].includes(id))document.getElementById('bn-tools')?.classList.add('active');
  if(id==='glossary')document.getElementById('bn-gloss')?.classList.add('active');
  window.scrollTo(0,0);
  updPtsDisplay();
  // Reposition morphing bnav indicator under active tab
  if(!isTitle) requestAnimationFrame(()=>positionBnavIndicator());
}
function positionBnavIndicator(){
  const bnav=document.getElementById('bnav');
  const ind=document.getElementById('bnavIndicator');
  if(!bnav||!ind) return;
  const active=bnav.querySelector('.bnav-btn.active');
  if(!active) return;
  const bnavRect=bnav.getBoundingClientRect();
  const btnRect=active.getBoundingClientRect();
  const offsetX=btnRect.left - bnavRect.left - 6; // subtract bnav padding (6px)
  const width=btnRect.width;
  ind.style.width=width+'px';
  ind.style.transform=`translateX(${offsetX}px)`;
}
window.addEventListener('resize',()=>{if(cur!=='title')positionBnavIndicator();});
function goHome(){hist=[];showS('home');renderHome();}
function goMenu(){hist.push(cur);curPath='all';document.getElementById('menuPathTitle').textContent='Всі модулі';showS('menu');renderMods();}
function goTools(){hist.push(cur);showS('tools');updToolsStats();}
function goCalc(){hist.push(cur);showS('calc');}
function goJournal(){hist.push(cur);showS('journal');renderJournal();}
function goSimulator(){hist.push(cur);showS('simulator');simInit();}
function goGloss(){hist.push(cur);showS('glossary');renderGloss();}
function goBack(){
  const p=hist.pop()||'home';
  showS(p);
  if(p==='home')renderHome();
  if(p==='menu')renderMods();
  if(p==='journal')renderJournal();
}

const PATH_MAP={
  beginner:['market-mechanics','risk-math','chart-anatomy'],
  smc:['structure','ob','fvg','liquidity','entry'],
  advanced:['killzones','mtf','amd','narrative','physics','macro','ipda','mitigation','wyckoff','retail-vs-smart','silver-bullet','breaker-block'],
  psych:['risk','psychology'],
};
const PATH_LABELS={beginner:'🌱 Початківець',smc:'📐 SMC Core',advanced:'🔥 Просунутий',psych:'🧠 Психологія'};

function openPath(path){
  hist.push('home');
  curPath=path;
  document.getElementById('menuPathTitle').textContent=PATH_LABELS[path]||'Модулі';
  showS('menu');
  renderMods();
}

function renderHome(){
  updPtsDisplay();
  const total=MODS.length;
  const pct=Math.round(done.size/total*100);

  // Stats strip
  document.getElementById('hstat-done').textContent=done.size;
  document.getElementById('hstat-pts').textContent=getPoints();
  document.getElementById('hstat-pct').textContent=pct+'%';

  // Progress ring (circumference = 2π×54 ≈ 339.29)
  const circ=339.29;
  const offset=circ-(circ*pct/100);
  const ring=document.getElementById('prog-ring');
  const ringPct=document.getElementById('ring-pct');
  if(ring){ ring.style.strokeDashoffset=offset; }
  if(ringPct){ ringPct.textContent=pct+'%'; }
  // Update trader level badge based on progress
  const lvlEl=document.querySelector('.progress-ring-level');
  if(lvlEl){
    let lvl='TRADER · LVL 1';
    if(pct>=100) lvl='⭐ MASTER · MAX';
    else if(pct>=75) lvl='💎 EXPERT · LVL 5';
    else if(pct>=50) lvl='🔥 PRO · LVL 4';
    else if(pct>=30) lvl='📈 SKILLED · LVL 3';
    else if(pct>=10) lvl='🎯 ROOKIE · LVL 2';
    lvlEl.textContent=lvl;
  }

  // Path progress bars
  Object.entries(PATH_MAP).forEach(([key,ids])=>{
    const cnt=ids.filter(id=>done.has(id)).length;
    const tot=ids.length;
    const fill=document.getElementById('pp-'+key);
    const txt=document.getElementById('ppt-'+key);
    if(fill) fill.style.width=(cnt/tot*100)+'%';
    if(txt) txt.textContent=cnt+' / '+tot+' модулів';
  });

  // Greeting
  const greet=done.size===0?'Обери свій шлях — починай з Фундаменту 🌱':
    pct>=100?'🎉 Всі модулі пройдено! Ти майстер SMC!':
    pct+'% пройдено · '+(MODS.length-done.size)+' модулів залишилось';
  document.getElementById('home-greeting').textContent=greet;
}

function updToolsStats(){
  const entries=ls('smc_journal',[]);
  document.getElementById('jrn-count-badge').textContent=entries.length+' угод';
  const simBest=ls('smc_sim_best',0);
  document.getElementById('sim-score-badge').textContent='Рекорд: '+simBest;
  document.getElementById('tools-stats-txt').textContent=`Завершено модулів: ${done.size} · Балів: ${getPoints()} · Угод у журналі: ${entries.length}`;
}

// ═══════════ MODULES ═══════════

let done=new Set(ls('smc_done',[]));
let quizDone=new Set(ls('smc_quiz_done',[])); // tracks which module quizzes completed

function renderMods(f=''){
  const ml=document.getElementById('modList'); ml.innerHTML='';
  let modsToShow=MODS;
  if(curPath&&curPath!=='all'){
    const ids=PATH_MAP[curPath]||[];
    modsToShow=MODS.filter(m=>ids.includes(m.id));
  }
  if(f) modsToShow=modsToShow.filter(m=>m.title.toLowerCase().includes(f.toLowerCase())||m.tags.some(t=>t.toLowerCase().includes(f.toLowerCase())));
  let lastSec='';
  modsToShow.forEach(m=>{
    if(m.sec&&m.sec!==lastSec){ml.innerHTML+=`<div class="menu-sec">${m.sec}</div>`;lastSec=m.sec;}
    const ok=done.has(m.id);
    const qok=quizDone.has(m.id);
    ml.innerHTML+=`<div class="mcard ${ok?'done':''}" onclick="openLesson('${m.id}')">
      <div class="mcard-shimmer"></div>
      <div class="mcard-bar"></div>
      <div class="mc-top">
        <div class="mc-icon" style="background:${m.col}">${m.icon}</div>
        <div class="mc-meta">
          <div class="mc-num">Модуль ${m.num}</div>
          <div class="mc-title">${m.title}</div>
          <div class="mc-desc">${m.desc}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="mc-badge ${qok?'mc-badge-star':ok?'mc-badge-done':''}" style="${qok||ok?'':`background:${m.bc};color:${m.bt}`}">${qok?'⭐':ok?'✓':m.badge}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="mc-bottom">
        <div class="mc-tags">${m.tags.map(t=>`<span class="mc-tag">${t}</span>`).join('')}</div>
        <div class="mc-count">${m.cnt} уроки ${qok?'· Тест ✓':''}</div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  });
  ml.innerHTML+='<div style="height:20px"></div>';
  updProg();
}
function filterMods(v){renderMods(v);}
function updProg(){
  const p=Math.round(done.size/MODS.length*100);
  document.getElementById('progFill').style.width=p+'%';
  document.getElementById('progTxt').textContent=p+'%';
  lsSave('smc_done',[...done]);
}

// ═══════════ LESSON ═══════════
let curLessonId='';
function openLesson(id){
  hist.push(cur==='home'?'home':'menu');
  curLessonId=id;
  const m=MODS.find(x=>x.id===id);
  document.getElementById('lessonTitle').textContent=m.title;
  document.getElementById('lessonNum').textContent=`Модуль ${m.num} · ${m.cnt} уроки`;
  showS('lesson');buildLesson(id);
  // Mark as visited (no points — points come from quiz)
  if(!done.has(id)){done.add(id);updProg();}
}
function buildLesson(id){
  const pages=PAGES[id]||[['Вступ','<p>Контент в розробці</p>']];
  document.getElementById('lessonTabs').innerHTML=pages.map((p,i)=>`<div class="ltab ${i===0?'active':''}" onclick="switchTab(${i})">${p[0]}</div>`).join('');
  document.getElementById('lessonContent').innerHTML=pages.map((p,i)=>`<div class="lpage ${i===0?'active':''}" id="lp-${i}">${p[1]}</div>`).join('');
  setTimeout(()=>document.querySelectorAll('canvas[data-draw]').forEach(c=>window[c.dataset.draw]?.(c)),80);
}
function switchTab(i){
  document.querySelectorAll('.ltab').forEach((t,ti)=>t.classList.toggle('active',ti===i));
  document.querySelectorAll('.lpage').forEach((p,pi)=>p.classList.toggle('active',pi===i));
  setTimeout(()=>document.querySelectorAll('canvas[data-draw]').forEach(c=>window[c.dataset.draw]?.(c)),60);
}

// ═══════════ CALCULATOR ═══════════
let calcRisk=1;
function setRisk(r){
  calcRisk=r;
  document.querySelectorAll('.risk-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('rsk-'+r)?.classList.add('active');
  calcUpdate();
}
function calcUpdate(){
  const dep=parseFloat(document.getElementById('c-deposit').value)||0;
  const entry=parseFloat(document.getElementById('c-entry').value)||0;
  const sl=parseFloat(document.getElementById('c-sl').value)||0;
  if(!dep||!entry||!sl||sl===entry){
    ['cr-risk','cr-slpct','cr-size','cr-qty','cr-tp1','cr-tp2'].forEach(id=>document.getElementById(id).textContent='—');
    return;
  }
  const riskAmt=dep*(calcRisk/100);
  const slPct=Math.abs((entry-sl)/entry*100);
  const posSize=riskAmt/slPct*100;
  const qty=posSize/entry;
  const slDiff=Math.abs(entry-sl);
  const bull=entry>sl;
  const tp1=bull?entry+slDiff*2:entry-slDiff*2;
  const tp2=bull?entry+slDiff*3:entry-slDiff*3;
  document.getElementById('cr-risk').textContent='$'+riskAmt.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('cr-slpct').textContent=slPct.toFixed(2)+'%';
  document.getElementById('cr-size').textContent='$'+posSize.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('cr-qty').textContent=qty.toFixed(6);
  document.getElementById('cr-tp1').textContent='$'+tp1.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('cr-tp2').textContent='$'+tp2.toFixed(2);
}

// ═══════════ JOURNAL ═══════════
let jDir='long', jResult='open';
function setDir(d){
  jDir=d;
  document.getElementById('jdir-long').className='dir-btn'+(d==='long'?' long-sel':'');
  document.getElementById('jdir-short').className='dir-btn'+(d==='short'?' short-sel':'');
}
function setJResult(r){
  jResult=r;
  ['win','loss','be','open'].forEach(x=>document.getElementById('jr-'+x).className='result-btn'+(r===x?' '+r+'-sel':''));
}
function openJrnSheet(){document.getElementById('jrn-overlay').classList.add('show');document.body.style.overflow='hidden';}
function closeJrnSheet(e){if(e.target===document.getElementById('jrn-overlay')){document.getElementById('jrn-overlay').classList.remove('show');document.body.style.overflow='';}}
function saveJrnEntry(){
  const pair=document.getElementById('js-pair').value.trim()||'BTC/USDT';
  const entry=parseFloat(document.getElementById('js-entry').value)||0;
  const sl=parseFloat(document.getElementById('js-sl').value)||0;
  const tp=parseFloat(document.getElementById('js-tp').value)||0;
  const reason=document.getElementById('js-reason').value.trim();
  const score=parseInt(document.getElementById('js-score').value)||5;
  const entries=ls('smc_journal',[]);
  let rr=0;
  if(entry&&sl&&tp){
    const risk=Math.abs(entry-sl);const reward=Math.abs(tp-entry);
    rr=risk?+(reward/risk).toFixed(1):0;
  }
  let pnl='—';
  if(jResult==='win'&&rr)pnl='+'+rr+'R';
  if(jResult==='loss')pnl='−1R';
  if(jResult==='be')pnl='0R';
  entries.unshift({id:Date.now(),pair,dir:jDir,entry,sl,tp,reason,score,result:jResult,rr,pnl,date:new Date().toLocaleDateString('uk-UA')});
  lsSave('smc_journal',entries);
  document.getElementById('jrn-overlay').classList.remove('show');
  document.body.style.overflow='';
  renderJournal();
  showToast('📓 Угоду збережено!');
  // reset
  ['js-pair','js-entry','js-sl','js-tp','js-reason','js-score'].forEach(id=>document.getElementById(id).value='');
  setDir('long');setJResult('open');
}

let jrnFilter='all';
function jrnTab(t){
  jrnFilter=t;
  ['all','win','loss'].forEach(x=>{document.getElementById('jt-'+x).classList.toggle('active',x===t);});
  renderJournal();
}
function renderJournal(){
  let entries=ls('smc_journal',[]);
  const wins=entries.filter(e=>e.result==='win').length;
  const losses=entries.filter(e=>e.result==='loss').length;
  const wr=entries.length?Math.round(wins/entries.filter(e=>e.result!=='open').length*100)||0:0;
  const body=document.getElementById('jrn-body');
  body.innerHTML=`<div class="jrn-stats">
    <div class="jstat"><div class="jstat-val g">${wins}</div><div class="jstat-lbl">Win</div></div>
    <div class="jstat"><div class="jstat-val r">${losses}</div><div class="jstat-lbl">Loss</div></div>
    <div class="jstat"><div class="jstat-val p">${wr}%</div><div class="jstat-lbl">Win Rate</div></div>
  </div>`;
  if(jrnFilter!=='all')entries=entries.filter(e=>e.result===jrnFilter);
  if(!entries.length){
    body.innerHTML+=`<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">📓</div><div class="empty-txt">Угод ще немає.<br>Натисни <strong>+</strong> щоб додати першу угоду.</div></div>`;
    return;
  }
  entries.forEach(e=>{
    const rc=e.result==='win'?'#26a69a':e.result==='loss'?'#ef5350':e.result==='be'?'#a78bfa':'#6b72a0';
    const rl=e.result==='win'?'✅ Win':e.result==='loss'?'❌ Loss':e.result==='be'?'➖ BE':'🔄 Open';
    body.innerHTML+=`<div class="jrn-entry">
      <div class="je-top">
        <div class="je-pair">${e.pair}</div>
        <div class="je-dir ${e.dir}">${e.dir==='long'?'📈 LONG':'📉 SHORT'}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="je-meta">
        <span>${e.date}</span>
        <span>Вхід: ${e.entry}</span>
        <span>SL: ${e.sl}</span>
        ${e.tp?`<span>TP: ${e.tp}</span>`:''}
      </div>
      ${e.reason?`<div class="je-reason">${e.reason}</div>`:''}
      <div class="je-result">
        <div class="je-rr" style="color:var(--muted2)">RR 1:${e.rr||'?'} · Оцінка: ${e.score}/8</div>
        <div class="je-pnl" style="color:${rc}">${rl} ${e.pnl&&e.pnl!='none'?('. '+e.pnl):''}</div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  });
}

// ═══════════ CHART SIMULATOR ═══════════
const SIM_PAIRS=['BTC/USDT','ETH/USDT','SOL/USDT'];
const SIM_TFS=['15M','1H','4H'];
let simState={correct:0,wrong:0,streak:0,total:0,answer:null,candles:[],revealCandles:[]};

function rng2(s){let x=Math.sin(s*9301+49297)*233280;return x-Math.floor(x);}
function genSimCandles(){
  const base=70+Math.floor(Math.random()*30);
  const n=20,bias=Math.random()>.5?.55:.45;
  let price=base,cs=[];
  const seed=Math.random()*9999;
  for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
    const r1=rng2(seed+i),r2=rng2(seed+i+100),r3=rng2(seed+i+200);
    const bull=r1<bias;
    const body=price*(0.008+r2*.025);
    const o=price,c=bull?o+body:o-body;
    const wu=body*(0.2+r3*.8),wd=body*(0.15+rng2(seed+i+300)*.7);
    cs.push({o,h:Math.max(o,c)+wu,l:Math.min(o,c)-wd,c,bull});
    price=c;
  }
  return cs;
}
function determineSimAnswer(candles){
  // Simple: look at last 5 candles structure
  const last=candles.slice(-5);
  const bulls=last.filter(c=>c.bull).length;
  const trend=candles[candles.length-1].c>candles[candles.length-5].c;
  const liq=candles[candles.length-1].l<Math.min(...candles.slice(-6,-1).map(c=>c.l));
  // if liq sweep + reversal pattern
  if(liq && candles[candles.length-1].bull){return{dir:'long',explain:'Ціна зробила sweep нижніх лоїв (SSL), зібрала ліквідність і закрилась бичачою свічкою — класичний розворот вгору. Великий гравець виконав покупки по стоп-лосах роздрібних трейдерів.'};}
  if(trend&&bulls>=3){return{dir:'long',explain:'Структура бичача: остання свічка закрилась вище попереднього хаю (BOS). Order Flow спрямований вгору — шукаємо лонг від найближчого Bullish OB.'};}
  if(!trend&&bulls<=2){return{dir:'short',explain:'Ведмежа структура підтверджена: ціна послідовно оновлює нижчі лої (LL) і хаї (LH). CHoCH зафіксовано — розумні гроші продають. Шукаємо шорт від Bearish OB.'};}
  const recent=candles.slice(-3);
  if(recent.every(c=>!c.bull)){return{dir:'short',explain:'Три ведмежі свічки поспіль — сильний імпульс продажу. Premium зона, FVG незаповнений нижче. Order Flow ведмежий.'};}
  return{dir:'long',explain:'Discount зона плюс бичача консолідація після корекції. Ціна тестує зону підтримки — потенційний Bullish OB. Чекаємо CHoCH на нижчому ТФ.'};
}
function simInit(){
  const cs=genSimCandles();
  simState.candles=cs.slice(0,15);
  simState.revealCandles=cs.slice(15);
  const ans=determineSimAnswer(cs);
  simState.answer=ans;
  const pi=Math.floor(Math.random()*SIM_PAIRS.length);
  const ti=Math.floor(Math.random()*SIM_TFS.length);
  document.getElementById('sim-pair-lbl').textContent=SIM_PAIRS[pi];
  document.getElementById('sim-tf-lbl').textContent=SIM_TFS[ti]+' · ??';
  document.getElementById('sim-btns').style.display='flex';
  document.getElementById('sim-result').classList.remove('show');
  simDrawChart(simState.candles,false);
  updSimScore();
}
function simDrawChart(candles,reveal){
  const canvas=document.getElementById('simCanvas');
  const W=canvas.parentElement.clientWidth;
  const H=200;const DPR=window.devicePixelRatio||1;
  canvas.width=W*DPR;canvas.height=H*DPR;canvas.style.width=W+'px';canvas.style.height=H+'px';
  const ctx=canvas.getContext('2d');ctx.scale(DPR,DPR);
  // App-themed gradient bg
  const grad=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
  grad.addColorStop(0,'#0c0d1c');grad.addColorStop(1,'#08091a');
  ctx.fillStyle=grad;ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  // purple grid
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(139,92,246,.05)';ctx.lineWidth=1;
  for(let y=0;y<H;y+=35){ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(0,y);ctx.lineTo(W,y);ctx.stroke();}
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(139,92,246,.035)';
  for(let x=0;x<W;x+=60){ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x,0);ctx.lineTo(x,H);ctx.stroke();}
  const all=reveal?[...candles,...simState.revealCandles.slice(0,5)]:candles;
  const mn=Math.min(...all.map(c=>c.l));const mx=Math.max(...all.map(c=>c.h));
  const range=mx-mn||1;const pad=14;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-mn)/range)*(H-pad*2);
  const cw=Math.floor((W-16)/all.length)-2;
  const step=cw+2,sx=8;
  const BULL='#00ff9d', BEAR='#ff3b5c', BEAR_EDGE='#ff5e7a', BULL_EDGE='#4dffb5';
  all.forEach((c,i)=>{
    const x=sx+i*step;
    const isReveal=reveal&&i>=candles.length;
    const bullC=isReveal?'rgba(0,255,157,.45)':BULL;
    const bearC=isReveal?'rgba(255,59,92,.45)':BEAR;
    const bearE=isReveal?'rgba(255,94,122,.5)':BEAR_EDGE;
    const bullE=isReveal?'rgba(77,255,181,.5)':BULL_EDGE;
    if(isReveal){ctx.setLineDash([2,2]);}else{ctx.setLineDash([]);}
    // wick
    ctx.strokeStyle=c.bull?bullE:bearE;ctx.lineWidth=1.2;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x+cw/2,toY(c.h));ctx.lineTo(x+cw/2,toY(c.l));ctx.stroke();
    ctx.setLineDash([]);
    const top=toY(Math.max(c.o,c.c)),bh=Math.max(1.5,Math.abs(toY(c.o)-toY(c.c)));
    ctx.fillStyle=c.bull?bullC:bearC;
    ctx.fillRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);
  });
  // Question mark area (purple glow)
  if(!reveal){
    const lastX=sx+candles.length*step;
    const qGrad=ctx.createLinearGradient(lastX,0,W,0);
    qGrad.addColorStop(0,'rgba(168,85,247,.06)');qGrad.addColorStop(1,'rgba(168,85,247,.22)');
    ctx.fillStyle=qGrad;ctx.fillRect(lastX,pad,W-lastX-8,H-pad*2);
    ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(168,85,247,.4)';ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.setLineDash([4,4]);
    ctx.strokeRect(lastX,pad,W-lastX-8,H-pad*2);ctx.setLineDash([]);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(192,132,252,.65)';ctx.font=`bold 32px 'Orbitron',sans-serif`;ctx.textAlign='center';
    ctx.fillText('?',lastX+(W-lastX-8)/2,H/2+10);
  }
}
function simGuess(dir){
  const correct=dir===simState.answer.dir;
  simState.total++;
  if(correct){simState.correct++;simState.streak++;addPoints(simState.streak>=3?10:5);}
  else{simState.wrong++;simState.streak=0;}
  const best=ls('smc_sim_best',0);
  if(simState.correct>best)lsSave('smc_sim_best',simState.correct);
  document.getElementById('sim-btns').style.display='none';
  simDrawChart(simState.candles,true);
  const title=correct?'✅ Правильно!':'❌ Неправильно';
  document.getElementById('sim-res-title').textContent=title;
  document.getElementById('sim-res-title').style.color=correct?'#00ff9d':'#ff3b5c';
  document.getElementById('sim-res-explain').textContent=simState.answer.explain;
  document.getElementById('sim-result').classList.add('show');
  updSimScore();
}
function simNext(){simInit();}
function updSimScore(){
  document.getElementById('sim-correct').textContent=simState.correct;
  document.getElementById('sim-wrong').textContent=simState.wrong;
  document.getElementById('sim-total').textContent=simState.total;
  document.getElementById('sim-streak').textContent=simState.streak+'🔥';
  document.getElementById('sim-pts-disp').textContent=getPoints();
}

// ═══════════ QUIZ ═══════════
function qA(btn,ok){
  if(btn.disabled) return;
  const box=btn.closest('.quiz-box');
  box.querySelectorAll('.quiz-opt').forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
  btn.classList.add(ok?'correct':'wrong');
  const reward=box.querySelector('.quiz-pts-reward');
  if(reward){
    reward.classList.add('show');
    reward.textContent=ok?'✅ Правильно!':'❌ Неправильно — перечитай урок.';
  }
  // After answering, check if whole test tab is done → award module completion bonus
  setTimeout(()=>{
    const page=btn.closest('.lpage');
    if(!page) return;
    const allBoxes=[...page.querySelectorAll('.quiz-box')];
    const allDone=allBoxes.every(b=>b.querySelector('.quiz-opt:disabled'));
    if(allDone && curLessonId && !quizDone.has(curLessonId)){
      const correct=allBoxes.filter(b=>b.querySelector('.quiz-opt.correct')).length;
      if(correct>0){
        quizDone.add(curLessonId);
        lsSave('smc_quiz_done',[...quizDone]);
        const bonus=correct===allBoxes.length?25:10;
        addPoints(bonus);
        showToast('🎓 Тест модуля завершено! +'+bonus+' балів'+(correct===allBoxes.length?' 🌟 Ідеально!':''));
      }
    }
  },300);
}


// ═══════════ CANVAS HELPERS ═══════════
const DPR=window.devicePixelRatio||1;
function setupC(c,h=200){
  const w=c.parentElement.clientWidth;
  c.width=w*DPR;c.height=h*DPR;c.style.width=w+'px';c.style.height=h+'px';
  const ctx=c.getContext('2d');ctx.scale(DPR,DPR);
  return{ctx,w,h};
}
function tvBg(ctx,w,h){
  // Hyper Edition chart background (deep space with neon grid)
  const grad=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,h);
  grad.addColorStop(0,'#070b20');grad.addColorStop(1,'#050815');
  ctx.fillStyle=grad;ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
  // subtle horizontal grid — cyan tint
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,234,255,.04)';ctx.lineWidth=1;
  for(let i=0;i<h;i+=40){ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(0,i);ctx.lineTo(w,i);ctx.stroke();}
  // even subtler vertical grid — purple
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(168,85,247,.04)';
  for(let i=0;i<w;i+=60){ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(i,0);ctx.lineTo(i,h);ctx.stroke();}
}
function cndl(ctx,x,o,c,hi,lo,cw,bull){
  // Hyper Edition: bullish = neon green (lime), bearish = neon red (crimson pink)
  const bullCol='#00ff9d', bearCol='#ff3b5c', bearEdge='#ff5e7a', bullEdge='#4dffb5';
  const col=bull?bullCol:bearCol;
  const wickCol=bull?bullEdge:bearEdge;
  ctx.strokeStyle=wickCol;ctx.fillStyle=col;ctx.lineWidth=1.2;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x+cw/2,hi);ctx.lineTo(x+cw/2,lo);ctx.stroke();
  const top=Math.min(o,c),bh=Math.max(1,Math.abs(c-o));
  ctx.fillRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);
}
function hl(ctx,y,x1,x2,col,dash=[]){ctx.save();ctx.strokeStyle=col;ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.setLineDash(dash);ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x1,y);ctx.lineTo(x2,y);ctx.stroke();ctx.restore();}
function zone(ctx,x1,y1,x2,y2,col,a=0.12){ctx.save();ctx.fillStyle=col;ctx.globalAlpha=a;ctx.fillRect(x1,y1,x2-x1,y2-y1);ctx.globalAlpha=1;ctx.strokeStyle=col;ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.strokeRect(x1,y1,x2-x1,y2-y1);ctx.restore();}
function txt(ctx,x,y,t,col,sz=8,align='center'){ctx.save();ctx.fillStyle=col;ctx.font=`bold ${sz}px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign=align;ctx.fillText(t,x,y);ctx.restore();}
function arr(ctx,x1,y1,x2,y2,col){ctx.save();ctx.strokeStyle=col;ctx.fillStyle=col;ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x1,y1);ctx.lineTo(x2,y2);ctx.stroke();const a=Math.atan2(y2-y1,x2-x1);ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x2,y2);ctx.lineTo(x2-7*Math.cos(a-.4),y2-7*Math.sin(a-.4));ctx.lineTo(x2-7*Math.cos(a+.4),y2-7*Math.sin(a+.4));ctx.closePath();ctx.fill();ctx.restore();}

// ═══════════ SPECIFIC DRAWS ═══════════
window.drawStructure=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,220);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=15,gap=5,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[200,190,205,183],[188,212,215,185],[210,198,215,195],[198,232,235,195],[230,218,235,214],[218,248,252,215],[246,230,250,225],[228,258,262,225],[256,238,262,230],[238,215,242,210],[213,195,218,192],[193,205,196,189],[204,192,208,188]];
  const minP=180,maxP=266,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-raw.length*step)/2;
  raw.forEach(([o,c,hi,lo],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(hi),toY(lo),cw,c>=o));
  [[3,210,'BOS'],[5,230,'BOS'],[7,248,'BOS']].forEach(([i,p,t])=>{hl(ctx,toY(p),sx+i*step,sx+(i+5)*step,'#8b5cf6',[4,4]);txt(ctx,sx+(i+5)*step+16,toY(p)+4,t,'#8b5cf6',9,'left');});
  hl(ctx,toY(238),sx+8*step,sx+12*step,'#fb923c',[4,4]);txt(ctx,sx+12*step+4,toY(238)+4,'CHoCH','#fb923c',9,'left');
  [[1,212,'HH'],[2,198,'HL'],[3,232,'HH'],[4,218,'HL'],[5,248,'HH'],[6,230,'HL'],[7,258,'HH'],[8,238,'HL'],[9,215,'LH']].forEach(([i,p,t])=>{const x=sx+i*step+cw/2,ih=t.endsWith('H')&&t!=='LH';txt(ctx,x,ih?toY(p)-9:toY(p)+16,t,t==='LH'?'#fb923c':'#6b72a0',8);});
};

window.drawRR=function(canvas){

  const pad=28,bw=50,gap=14,chartH=h-pad*2;

    ctx.fillStyle='#6b72a0';ctx.font=`9px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.fillText(l,x+bw/2,pad+chartH+15);
  });
};

window.drawPO3=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,180);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=20;
  const pts=[{label:'Open',x:.05,y:.5,col:'#e8edf8'},{label:'Sweep Low\n(Manipulation)',x:.35,y:.78,col:'#ef5350'},{label:'Mark Up',x:.65,y:.25,col:'#26a69a'},{label:'Close High',x:.9,y:.22,col:'#8b5cf6'}];

  ctx.strokeStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.lineWidth=2;ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx(pts[0].x),cy(pts[0].y));
  ctx.bezierCurveTo(cx(.2),cy(.6),cx(.25),cy(.85),cx(pts[1].x),cy(pts[1].y));
  ctx.bezierCurveTo(cx(.45),cy(.65),cx(.55),cy(.3),cx(pts[2].x),cy(pts[2].y));
  ctx.lineTo(cx(pts[3].x),cy(pts[3].y));ctx.stroke();
  pts.forEach(p=>{
    ctx.fillStyle=p.col;ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(cx(p.x),cy(p.y),4,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();
    const lines=p.label.split('\n');
    lines.forEach((l,li)=>txt(ctx,cx(p.x),cy(p.y)+(p.y>.5?18:-(lines.length-li)*12)+li*12,l,p.col,8));
  });
  txt(ctx,cx(.2),cy(.95),'① Consolidation','#5b9fff',8);
  txt(ctx,cx(.5),cy(.95),'② Manipulation','#ef5350',8);
  txt(ctx,cx(.78),cy(.95),'③ Distribution','#8b5cf6',8);
};

window.drawOrderBook=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,180);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const mid=h/2,pad=16;
  const bids=[80,65,50,38,28,18,10],asks=[75,60,48,36,25,15,8];
  const maxV=80,barH=18;
  bids.forEach((v,i)=>{const bw=(v/maxV)*(w/2-pad-4);ctx.fillStyle='rgba(38,166,154,.2)';ctx.fillRect(w/2-4-bw,mid-(i+1)*barH+2,bw,barH-2);ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(38,166,154,.4)';ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.strokeRect(w/2-4-bw,mid-(i+1)*barH+2,bw,barH-2);});
  asks.forEach((v,i)=>{const bw=(v/maxV)*(w/2-pad-4);ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.2)';ctx.fillRect(w/2+4,mid+i*barH+2,bw,barH-2);ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.4)';ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.strokeRect(w/2+4,mid+i*barH+2,bw,barH-2);});
  hl(ctx,mid,pad,w-pad,'#6b72a0');
  txt(ctx,w/2,mid-3,'СПРЕД','#6b72a0',8);
  txt(ctx,pad,mid-50,'Bids (Купівля)','#26a69a',8,'left');txt(ctx,w-pad,mid+35,'Asks (Продаж)','#ef5350',8,'right');
};

window.drawCorrelation=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,180);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=24,chartW=w-pad*2,chartH=h-pad*2-20;
  // BTC line (blue)
  const btc=[50,52,55,53,58,60,57,62,65,68,64,70,74];
  // Gold line (yellow) - slight positive correlation
  const gold=[48,49,52,51,54,56,53,58,60,62,59,64,67];
  // DXY (red) - inverse
  const dxy=[60,59,57,58,55,53,56,51,49,47,50,45,42];
  const n=btc.length,xStep=chartW/(n-1);
  const norm=(arr,mn,mx)=>arr.map(v=>pad+chartH-(v-mn)/(mx-mn)*chartH);
  const btcY=norm(btc,40,80);const goldY=norm(gold,40,80);const dxyY=norm(dxy,38,68);
  [[btcY,'#5b9fff','BTC'],[goldY,'#fbbf24','Gold'],[dxyY,'#ef5350','DXY']].forEach(([pts,col,label])=>{
    ctx.strokeStyle=col;ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.beginPath();
    pts.forEach((y,i)=>{const x=pad+i*xStep;i===0?ctx.moveTo(x,y):ctx.lineTo(x,y);});
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle=col;ctx.font=`bold 8px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='right';
    ctx.fillText(label,w-6,pts[pts.length-1]+3);
  });
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'Кореляція: BTC ↑ Gold ↑ · DXY ↓','#6b72a0',8);
};

window.drawFearGreed=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,160);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cx=w/2,cy=h*.62,r=Math.min(w,h)*.38;
  // Semicircle gauge
  const zones=[{from:Math.PI,to:Math.PI*1.2,col:'#ef5350',lbl:'Екстремальний\nстрах'},{from:Math.PI*1.2,to:Math.PI*1.4,col:'#fb923c',lbl:'Страх'},{from:Math.PI*1.4,to:Math.PI*1.6,col:'#fbbf24',lbl:'Нейтрально'},{from:Math.PI*1.6,to:Math.PI*1.8,col:'#a3e635',lbl:'Жадібність'},{from:Math.PI*1.8,to:Math.PI*2,col:'#26a69a',lbl:'Екстремальна\nжадібність'}];
  zones.forEach(z=>{
    ctx.strokeStyle=z.col;ctx.lineWidth=14;ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(cx,cy,r,z.from,z.to);ctx.stroke();
  });
  // Needle at ~65 (Greed)
  const val=65;const angle=Math.PI+(val/100)*Math.PI;
  ctx.strokeStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.lineWidth=2;ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx,cy);ctx.lineTo(cx+Math.cos(angle)*(r-10),cy+Math.sin(angle)*(r-10));ctx.stroke();
  ctx.fillStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(cx,cy,5,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle='#a3e635';ctx.font=`bold 22px 'Bebas Neue'`;ctx.textAlign='center';ctx.fillText('65',cx,cy-16);
  ctx.fillStyle='#a3e635';ctx.font=`bold 9px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.fillText('ЖАДІБНІСТЬ',cx,cy-4);
  txt(ctx,cx,h-4,'Fear & Greed Index — зараз 65/100','#6b72a0',8);
};
const H=(tag,title,text)=>`<div class="l-hero"><div class="l-tag">${tag}</div><div class="l-title">${title}</div><div class="l-text">${text}</div></div>`;
const IB=(cls,title,desc)=>`<div class="ibox ${cls}"><div class="ib-t">${title}</div><div class="ib-d">${desc}</div></div>`;
const TV=(pair,tf,legend,draw,h=220)=>`<div class="tv-chart"><div class="tv-topbar"><div><span class="tv-pair">${pair}</span><span class="tv-tf">${tf}</span></div><div class="tv-legend">${legend.map(([d,c])=>`<div class="tv-leg"><div class="tv-dot" style="background:${c}"></div>${d}</div>`).join('')}</div></div><canvas class="tv-canvas" height="${h}" data-draw="${draw}"></canvas></div>`;
const QZ=(q,opts,ci)=>`<div class="quiz-box"><div class="quiz-q">${q}</div><div class="quiz-opts">${opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="quiz-opt" onclick="qA(this,${i===ci})">${o}</button>`).join('')}</div><div class="quiz-pts-reward"></div></div>`;

window.drawBOSDetail=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,210);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[100,108],[107,115],[114,107],[106,113],[112,120],[119,112],[111,119],[118,126],[125,118],[117,124],[123,131],[130,122],[121,128]];
  const minP=97,maxP=135,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=pad;
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(Math.max(o,c)+1.5),toY(Math.min(o,c)-1),cw,c>=o));
  // BOS levels
  [[2,108,'HL'],[4,115,'HH'],[6,112,'HL'],[8,120,'HH'],[10,118,'HL'],[12,126,'HH']].forEach(([i,p,l])=>{
    const col=l==='HH'?'#26a69a':'#5b9fff';
    txt(ctx,sx+i*step+cw/2,toY(p)+(l==='HH'?-7:13),l,col,8);
  });
  [[4,115,'BOS'],[8,120,'BOS'],[12,126,'BOS']].forEach(([i,p])=>{
    hl(ctx,toY(p),sx+(i-2)*step,sx+(i+2)*step,'rgba(139,92,246,.5)',[3,4]);
    txt(ctx,sx+(i+2)*step+4,toY(p)-5,'BOS','#8b5cf6',8,'left');
  });
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'Серія BOS ↑ = підтвердження висхідного тренду','#6b72a0',8);
};

window.drawPremDiscFib=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=20,cw2=w-pad*2,ch=h-pad*2;
  const swing_lo=0.78,swing_hi=0.12;
  const yLo=pad+swing_lo*ch,yHi=pad+swing_hi*ch,yMid=(yLo+yHi)/2;
  const yD25=pad+(swing_lo-(swing_lo-swing_hi)*0.25)*ch;
  const yP75=pad+(swing_lo-(swing_lo-swing_hi)*0.75)*ch;
  // zones
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.07)';ctx.fillRect(pad,yHi,cw2,yMid-yHi);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(251,191,36,.04)';ctx.fillRect(pad,yMid-1,cw2,2);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(38,166,154,.07)';ctx.fillRect(pad,yMid,cw2,yLo-yMid);
  // Deep zones
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.1)';ctx.fillRect(pad,yHi,cw2,yP75-yHi);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(38,166,154,.1)';ctx.fillRect(pad,yD25,cw2,yLo-yD25);
  [yHi,yP75,yMid,yD25,yLo].forEach((y,i)=>{
    hl(ctx,y,pad,pad+cw2,[yHi,yP75,yMid,yD25,yLo].map((_,j)=>j===i?'#e8edf8':'#1e2040')[i],[]);
    const labels=['0% (BSL)','0.25 (Fib)','0.5 — Equilibrium','0.75 (Fib)','1.0 (SSL)'];
    const cols=['#fbbf24','#fb923c','#fbbf24','#26a69a','#fbbf24'];
    txt(ctx,pad+cw2-4,y-4,labels[i],cols[i],7,'right');
  });
  // Labels
  txt(ctx,pad+8,yHi+(yP75-yHi)/2,'🔴 Premium','#ef5350',9,'left');
  txt(ctx,pad+8,yD25+(yLo-yD25)/2,'🟢 Discount','#26a69a',9,'left');
  txt(ctx,pad+8,yMid-3,'── Equilibrium 50% ──','#fbbf24',7,'left');
  // Arrows
  arr(ctx,pad+cw2-60,yLo-8,pad+cw2-60,yHi+8,'rgba(38,166,154,.4)');
};

// ── FVG MODULE ────────────────────────────────────
window.drawFVGBearish=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,195);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[120,112],[111,103],[102,112],[111,120],[119,111],[110,118],[117,124],[123,115],[114,107],[106,114]];
  const minP=100,maxP=128,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=pad;
  // Bearish FVG — top of candle[0] > bottom of candle[2] (inverted)
  const fy1=toY(112),fy2=toY(103); // between candle 0 high and candle 2 low
  zone(ctx,sx+1*step,fy2,sx+6*step,fy1,'#ef5350',0.1);
  hl(ctx,fy1,sx+1*step,sx+6*step,'#ef5350',[4,4]);hl(ctx,fy2,sx+1*step,sx+6*step,'#ef5350',[4,4]);
  hl(ctx,(fy1+fy2)/2,sx+1*step,sx+6*step,'rgba(239,83,80,.25)',[2,5]);
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(Math.max(o,c)+1.5),toY(Math.min(o,c)-1),cw,c>=o));

  });

// ── RISK-MATH MODULE ──────────────────────────────
window.drawDrawdownComparison=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,195);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=20,barW=55,gap=18,ch=h-pad*2-30;
  const scenarios=[
    {risk:1,losses:10,after:90.4,col:'#26a69a',lbl:'Ризик 1%'},
    {risk:5,losses:10,after:59.9,col:'#fbbf24',lbl:'Ризик 5%'},
    {risk:10,losses:10,after:34.9,col:'#ef5350',lbl:'Ризик 10%'},
  ];
  const totalW=scenarios.length*(barW+gap)-gap;
  const sx=(w-totalW)/2;
  scenarios.forEach((s,i)=>{
    const x=sx+i*(barW+gap);
    // After bar
    const bh=s.after/100*ch;
    ctx.fillStyle=s.col;ctx.globalAlpha=.2;ctx.fillRect(x,pad+ch-bh,barW,bh);ctx.globalAlpha=1;
    ctx.strokeStyle=s.col;ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.strokeRect(x,pad+ch-bh,barW,bh);
    // Remaining label
    ctx.fillStyle=s.col;ctx.font=`bold 12px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='center';
    ctx.fillText(s.after.toFixed(0)+'%',x+barW/2,pad+ch-bh-5);
    // Bottom label
    ctx.fillStyle=s.col;ctx.font=`9px 'JetBrains Mono'`;
    ctx.fillText(s.lbl,x+barW/2,pad+ch+14);
    ctx.fillStyle='#6b72a0';ctx.font=`8px 'JetBrains Mono'`;
    ctx.fillText('10 збитків',x+barW/2,pad+ch+26);
  });
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'Залишок рахунку після 10 збиткових угод підряд','#6b72a0',8);
};

  // Visual: deposit → risk 1% → position size
  const boxes=[
    {lbl:'Депозит',val:'$1,000',col:'#5b9fff',x:0.02,w:0.96,y:0.05,h:0.22},
    {lbl:'Ризик 1%',val:'$10',col:'#ef5350',x:0.02,w:0.10,y:0.40,h:0.22},
    {lbl:'SL відстань 1.5%',val:'$15',col:'#fb923c',x:0.14,w:0.20,y:0.40,h:0.22},
    {lbl:'Розмір позиції',val:'$667',col:'#26a69a',x:0.36,w:0.62,y:0.40,h:0.22},
  ];
  const cw2=w-pad*2,ch=h-pad*2;
  boxes.forEach(b=>{
    const x=pad+b.x*cw2,y=pad+b.y*ch,bw=b.w*cw2,bh=b.h*ch;
    ctx.fillStyle=b.col;ctx.globalAlpha=.12;ctx.fillRect(x,y,bw,bh);ctx.globalAlpha=1;
    ctx.strokeStyle=b.col;ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.strokeRect(x,y,bw,bh);
    txt(ctx,x+bw/2,y+bh/2-5,b.lbl,b.col,8);
    txt(ctx,x+bw/2,y+bh/2+8,b.val,b.col,10);
  });
  // Formula arrow
  arr(ctx,pad+0.55*cw2,pad+0.30*ch,pad+0.67*cw2,pad+0.38*ch,'rgba(38,166,154,.4)');
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'Позиція = Ризик ÷ SL%  →  $10 ÷ 1.5% = $667','#6b72a0',8);
};

window.drawJournalChart=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,185);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=18;
  // Simulated equity curve with journal
  const trades=[0,3,-1,4,5,-1,2,6,-2,4,7,-1,3,8,5,9,11,8,12];
  let equity=100,prev=100;
  const n=trades.length;
  const minE=80,maxE=115,range=maxE-minE;
  const toY=e=>pad+(1-(e-minE)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const xStep=(w-pad*2)/(n-1);
  // Draw equity line
  ctx.strokeStyle='#8b5cf6';ctx.lineWidth=2;ctx.beginPath();
  trades.forEach((t,i)=>{
    equity=100+t*0.8;
    const x=pad+i*xStep,y=toY(equity);
    i===0?ctx.moveTo(x,y):ctx.lineTo(x,y);
  });ctx.stroke();
  // Fill under
  equity=100;
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(139,92,246,.08)';ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(pad,toY(100));
  trades.forEach((t,i)=>{equity=100+t*0.8;ctx.lineTo(pad+i*xStep,toY(equity));});
  ctx.lineTo(pad+(n-1)*xStep,h-pad);ctx.lineTo(pad,h-pad);ctx.closePath();ctx.fill();
  // Baseline
  hl(ctx,toY(100),pad,w-pad,'rgba(255,255,255,.15)',[3,4]);
  txt(ctx,pad+4,toY(100)-5,'Стартовий депозит','#6b72a0',7,'left');
  // Win/Loss dots
  trades.forEach((t,i)=>{
    if(t===0)return;
    equity=100+t*0.8;
    ctx.fillStyle=t>0?'#26a69a':'#ef5350';
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(pad+i*xStep,toY(equity),3,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();
  });
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'Equity curve з веденням журналу = стабільне зростання','#6b72a0',8);
};

// ── NARRATIVE MODULE ──────────────────────────────
window.drawOrderFlowViz=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,210);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[100,108],[107,115],[114,106],[105,112],[111,119],[118,110],[109,116],[115,123],[122,115],[114,121],[120,128]];
  const minP=97,maxP=133,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=pad;
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(Math.max(o,c)+1.5),toY(Math.min(o,c)-1),cw,c>=o));
  // BOS arrows showing order flow direction
  [[2,106,'HL'],[4,111,'HH→BOS'],[6,109,'HL'],[8,115,'HH→BOS'],[10,120,'HL']].forEach(([i,p,l])=>{
    const col=l.includes('BOS')?'#8b5cf6':'#5b9fff';
    const up=l.includes('HH');
    if(up){
      arr(ctx,sx+i*step+cw/2,toY(p)+8,sx+i*step+cw/2,toY(p)-6,col);
      txt(ctx,sx+i*step+cw+2,toY(p)-4,l,col,7,'left');
    }else{
      txt(ctx,sx+i*step+cw/2,toY(p)+14,l,col,7);
    }
  });
  // Flow arrow
  arr(ctx,sx+1*step,toY(100),sx+10*step,toY(100),'rgba(38,166,154,.2)');
  txt(ctx,sx+5*step+cw/2,toY(100)+14,'Bullish Order Flow →','#26a69a',8);
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'HTF BOS серія вгору = Bullish Order Flow = тільки лонги','#6b72a0',8);
};

window.drawPatternVsNarrative=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,190);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=11,gap=3,step=cw+gap,pad=18;
  const half=Math.floor((w-pad*2-12)/2);
  // LEFT: Pattern-only (wrong — shows isolated OB without context)
  const lPrices=[[110,102],[101,109],[108,100],[99,107],[106,114],[113,106],[105,112]];
  const toYL=p=>{const mn=96,mx=118;return pad+(1-(p-mn)/(mx-mn))*(h-pad*2);};
  zone(ctx,pad+2*step,toYL(110),pad+half,toYL(102),'#5b9fff',0.1);
  lPrices.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,pad+i*step,toYL(o),toYL(c),toYL(Math.max(o,c)+1.5),toYL(Math.min(o,c)-1),cw,c>=o));
  // Wrong entry with X
  ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.lineWidth=2;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(pad+5*step-4,pad+0.3*(h-pad*2)-4);ctx.lineTo(pad+5*step+cw+4,pad+0.3*(h-pad*2)+12);
  ctx.moveTo(pad+5*step+cw+4,pad+0.3*(h-pad*2)-4);ctx.lineTo(pad+5*step-4,pad+0.3*(h-pad*2)+12);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,pad+half/2,pad+6,'❌ Паттерн без контексту','#ef5350',8);
  txt(ctx,pad+half/2,h-4,'"Бачу OB → входжу"','#6b72a0',7);
  // RIGHT: Narrative (correct)
  const rPrices=[[100,107],[106,115],[114,106],[105,112],[111,120],[119,111],[110,117]];
  const toYR=p=>{const mn=97,mx=124;return pad+(1-(p-mn)/(mx-mn))*(h-pad*2);};
  const rx=pad+half+12;
  zone(ctx,rx+3*step,toYR(114),rx+half,toYR(106),'#5b9fff',0.12);
  hl(ctx,toYR(106),rx,rx+half,'#fbbf24',[3,4]);txt(ctx,rx+4,toYR(106)+11,'SSL swept','#fbbf24',7,'left');
  rPrices.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,rx+i*step,toYR(o),toYR(c),toYR(Math.max(o,c)+1.5),toYR(Math.min(o,c)-1),cw,c>=o));
  arr(ctx,rx+5*step+cw/2,toYR(107),rx+5*step+cw/2,toYR(113),'#26a69a');
  txt(ctx,rx+half/2,pad+6,'✅ Narrative + контекст','#26a69a',8);
  txt(ctx,rx+half/2,h-4,'HTF↑+Discount+IDM+KZ','#26a69a',7);
  ctx.strokeStyle='#1e2040';ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(pad+half+6,pad);ctx.lineTo(pad+half+6,h-8);ctx.stroke();
};

// ── PSYCHOLOGY MODULE ─────────────────────────────
window.drawEmotionCycle=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cx=w/2,cy=h/2,r=Math.min(w,h)*0.35;
  const emotions=[
    {label:'Надія',angle:-Math.PI*0.75,col:'#5b9fff'},
    {label:'Оптимізм',angle:-Math.PI*0.5,col:'#26a69a'},
    {label:'Ейфорія ⚠️',angle:-Math.PI*0.25,col:'#fbbf24'},
    {label:'Тривога',angle:0,col:'#fb923c'},
    {label:'Паніка ⚠️',angle:Math.PI*0.25,col:'#ef5350'},
    {label:'Депресія',angle:Math.PI*0.5,col:'#ef5350'},
    {label:'Капітуляція ⭐',angle:Math.PI*0.75,col:'#8b5cf6'},
    {label:'Зневіра',angle:Math.PI,col:'#6b72a0'},
  ];
  // Price curve around circle
  ctx.strokeStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.lineWidth=2;ctx.beginPath();
  for(let a=-Math.PI;a<=Math.PI;a+=0.05){
    const pr=r*(0.7+0.3*Math.sin(a*2));
    const x=cx+pr*Math.cos(a),y=cy+pr*Math.sin(a);
    a===-Math.PI?ctx.moveTo(x,y):ctx.lineTo(x,y);
  }ctx.stroke();
  emotions.forEach(e=>{
    const x=cx+(r+20)*Math.cos(e.angle),y=cy+(r+20)*Math.sin(e.angle);
    ctx.fillStyle=e.col;ctx.font=`bold 8px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='center';ctx.fillText(e.label,x,y+3);
  });
  txt(ctx,cx,cy,'Цикл ринкових емоцій','#6b72a0',9);
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-6,'Ейфорія = продавати. Капітуляція = купувати.','#6b72a0',7);
};

window.drawDisciplineChart=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,185);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=20;
  // Two equity curves: with & without discipline
  const n=16;
  const goodTrades=[0,2,-1,3,2,-1,4,3,-1,3,4,2,-1,5,4,6];
  const badTrades=[0,5,-8,12,-15,3,-9,6,2,-12,8,-10,4,-7,5,2];
  let ge=100,be=100;
  const minE=30,maxE=140,range=maxE-minE;
  const xStep=(w-pad*2)/(n-1);
  const toY=e=>pad+(1-(e-minE)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  // Bad (undisciplined)
  ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.beginPath();
  badTrades.forEach((t,i)=>{be=Math.max(5,be+t*0.8);const x=pad+i*xStep;i===0?ctx.moveTo(x,toY(be)):ctx.lineTo(x,toY(be));});
  ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,w-pad-4,toY(be)+3,'Без дисципліни','#ef5350',7,'right');
  // Good (disciplined)
  ge=100;ctx.strokeStyle='#26a69a';ctx.lineWidth=2;ctx.beginPath();
  goodTrades.forEach((t,i)=>{ge=Math.max(80,ge+t*0.8);const x=pad+i*xStep;i===0?ctx.moveTo(x,toY(ge)):ctx.lineTo(x,toY(ge));});
  ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,w-pad-4,toY(ge)-8,'З дисципліною','#26a69a',7,'right');
  // Baseline
  hl(ctx,toY(100),pad,w-pad,'rgba(255,255,255,.12)',[4,4]);
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-5,'Дисципліна = стабільний ріст. Без неї = рандомний результат','#6b72a0',7);
};

window.drawTradingRoutine=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,185);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=14;
  const steps=[
    {t:'18:00–18:30',a:'Weekly + Daily: HTF Narrative, незакриті зони',col:'#fbbf24'},
    {t:'18:30–19:15',a:'4H: BOS підтвердження, OB+FVG, ліквідність',col:'#fb923c'},
    {t:'19:15–19:45',a:'1H/15M: Є сигнал? Killzone активна? → ордер',col:'#8b5cf6'},
    {t:'19:45–20:00',a:'Журнал: результат дня + що можна покращити',col:'#26a69a'},
  ];
  const bh=30,gap=5;
  steps.forEach((s,i)=>{
    const y=pad+i*(bh+gap);
    ctx.fillStyle=s.col;ctx.globalAlpha=.1;ctx.fillRect(pad,y,w-pad*2,bh);ctx.globalAlpha=1;
    ctx.strokeStyle=s.col;ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.strokeRect(pad,y,w-pad*2,bh);
    ctx.fillStyle=s.col;ctx.font=`bold 9px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='left';
    ctx.fillText(s.t,pad+6,y+12);
    ctx.fillStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.font=`8px 'Manrope'`;
    ctx.fillText(s.a,pad+90,y+12);
    // Progress dot
    ctx.fillStyle=s.col;ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(pad+80,y+bh/2,4,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();
  });
  // Connecting line
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.1)';ctx.lineWidth=1;
  for(let i=0;i<steps.length-1;i++){
    const y1=pad+i*(bh+gap)+bh/2,y2=pad+(i+1)*(bh+gap)+bh/2;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(pad+80,y1+4);ctx.lineTo(pad+80,y2-4);ctx.stroke();
  }
};

// ── IPDA MODULE ────────────────────────────────────
window.drawIPDALevels=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,195);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=18;
  const cw2=w-pad*2,ch=h-pad*2;
  // Level lines
  const levels=[
    {y:0.08,lbl:'Weekly BSL (ціль #1)',col:'#fbbf24',dash:[6,4]},
    {y:0.22,lbl:'Daily OB (незаповнений)',col:'#fb923c',dash:[4,4]},
    {y:0.42,lbl:'Поточна ціна ▼',col:'#e8edf8',dash:[]},
    {y:0.60,lbl:'4H FVG (зона входу)',col:'#8b5cf6',dash:[3,4]},
    {y:0.75,lbl:'Daily SSL (IDM ціль)',col:'#ef5350',dash:[5,3]},
    {y:0.90,lbl:'Weekly SSL (ціль #2)',col:'#fbbf24',dash:[6,4]},
  ];
  levels.forEach(l=>{
    const y=pad+l.y*ch;
    ctx.strokeStyle=l.col;ctx.lineWidth=l.dash.length?1:2;ctx.setLineDash(l.dash);
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(pad,y);ctx.lineTo(w-pad,y);ctx.stroke();ctx.setLineDash([]);
    txt(ctx,pad+4,y-4,l.lbl,l.col,8,'left');
  });
  const curY=pad+0.42*ch;
  ctx.fillStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(w/2,curY,5,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();
  // Arrows
  arr(ctx,w-40,curY-8,w-40,pad+0.10*ch,'rgba(251,191,36,.4)');
  arr(ctx,w-60,curY+8,w-60,pad+0.73*ch,'rgba(239,83,80,.3)');
};

// ── MITIGATION MODULE ──────────────────────────────
window.drawMitigationProcess=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=20;
  const steps=[
    {x:0.05,y:0.15,w:0.18,h:0.3,lbl:'1. Банк відкриває\nвеликий SELL',col:'#ef5350'},
    {x:0.28,y:0.15,w:0.18,h:0.3,lbl:'2. Ціна падає →\nформується OB',col:'#fb923c'},
    {x:0.51,y:0.15,w:0.18,h:0.3,lbl:'3. Ціна повертається\nдо OB (Mitigation)',col:'#fbbf24'},
    {x:0.74,y:0.15,w:0.18,h:0.3,lbl:'4. Банк закриває\nDrawdown → SELL↑',col:'#26a69a'},
  ];
  const cw2=w-pad*2,ch=h-pad*2;
  steps.forEach((s,i)=>{
    const x=pad+s.x*cw2,y=pad+s.y*ch,bw=s.w*cw2,bh=s.h*ch;
    ctx.fillStyle=s.col;ctx.globalAlpha=.1;ctx.fillRect(x,y,bw,bh);ctx.globalAlpha=1;
    ctx.strokeStyle=s.col;ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.strokeRect(x,y,bw,bh);
    const lines=s.lbl.split('\n');
    lines.forEach((l,li)=>{
      ctx.fillStyle=s.col;ctx.font=`bold 8px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='center';
      ctx.fillText(l,x+bw/2,y+bh/2+(li-0.5)*12);
    });
    if(i<steps.length-1) arr(ctx,x+bw+4,y+bh/2,pad+(steps[i+1].x)*cw2-4,y+bh/2,s.col);
  });
  // Price path
  ctx.strokeStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.lineWidth=2;ctx.beginPath();
  [[0.14,0.5],[0.37,0.8],[0.60,0.6],[0.83,0.75]].forEach(([px,py],i)=>{
    const x=pad+px*cw2,y=pad+py*ch;
    i===0?ctx.moveTo(x,y):ctx.lineTo(x,y);
  });ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-5,'Процес мітигації: банк повертає ціну щоб закрити DrawDown','#6b72a0',8);
};

// ── SILVER BULLET MODULE ───────────────────────────
window.drawSilverBulletTimes=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,180);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=14;
  // 24-hour timeline with 3 Silver Bullet windows (NY time converted to UTC+2 Kyiv)
  // NY 03-04 = Kyiv 10-11, NY 10-11 = Kyiv 17-18, NY 14-15 = Kyiv 21-22
  const cw2=w-pad*2,hourW=cw2/24;
  const windows=[
    {start:10,end:11,name:'London Open SB',col:'#8b5cf6'},
    {start:17,end:18,name:'NY AM SB',col:'#fb923c'},
    {start:21,end:22,name:'NY PM SB',col:'#ec407a'},
  ];
  // Draw hour grid
  for(let i=0;i<=24;i+=2){
    const x=pad+i*hourW;
    ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.08)';ctx.lineWidth=1;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x,pad+15);ctx.lineTo(x,h-30);ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle='#2a2a2a';ctx.font=`7px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='center';
    ctx.fillText(i.toString().padStart(2,'0'),x,h-18);
  }
  // Main timeline bar
  ctx.fillStyle='#2a2a2a';ctx.fillRect(pad,pad+22,cw2,6);
  // Draw windows
  windows.forEach((win,i)=>{
    const x=pad+win.start*hourW;const bw=(win.end-win.start)*hourW;
    ctx.fillStyle=win.col;ctx.fillRect(x,pad+22,bw,6);
    // Flag above
    ctx.fillStyle=win.col;ctx.fillRect(x-1,pad+8,bw+2,16);
    ctx.fillStyle='#fff';ctx.font=`bold 8px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='center';
    ctx.fillText(win.name,x+bw/2,pad+19);
    // Time label below
    ctx.fillStyle=win.col;ctx.font=`bold 9px 'JetBrains Mono'`;
    ctx.fillText(win.start+':00',x+bw/2,pad+42);
  });
  ctx.fillStyle='#1a1a1a';ctx.font=`bold 8px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='left';
  ctx.fillText('Київ (UTC+2) · 3 Silver Bullet вікна',pad,h-4);
};

window.drawSilverBulletSetup=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,215);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=12,gap=3,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[100,104],[103,108],[107,112],[111,106],[105,101],[100,96],[95,99],[98,103],[102,107],[106,111],[110,108],[107,110],[109,114],[113,118],[117,115]];
  const minP=92,maxP=122,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=pad;
  // SSL liquidity
  hl(ctx,toY(100),sx,w-pad,'#fbbf24',[4,3]);txt(ctx,sx+4,toY(100)-6,'SSL','#fbbf24',8,'left');
  // Sweep
  txt(ctx,sx+5*step+cw/2,toY(96)+14,'1. Sweep','#ec407a',8);
  // MSS level after sweep
  hl(ctx,toY(103),sx+6*step,sx+10*step,'#8b5cf6',[3,4]);txt(ctx,sx+7*step,toY(103)-6,'2. MSS','#8b5cf6',8);
  // FVG zone
  zone(ctx,sx+9*step,toY(109),sx+12*step,toY(106),'#8b5cf6',0.15);
  txt(ctx,sx+10*step,toY(109)-6,'3. FVG','#8b5cf6',8);
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(Math.max(o,c)+1.2),toY(Math.min(o,c)-0.8),cw,c>=o));
  // Entry arrow
  arr(ctx,sx+11*step+cw/2,toY(108),sx+11*step+cw/2,toY(115),'#ec407a');
  txt(ctx,sx+11*step+cw+4,toY(112),'4. Entry','#ec407a',8,'left');
  // SL + TP
  hl(ctx,toY(95),sx+11*step,w-pad,'#1a1a1a',[3,4]);txt(ctx,w-pad-4,toY(95)+11,'SL','#1a1a1a',8,'right');
  hl(ctx,toY(120),sx+11*step,w-pad,'#26a69a',[3,4]);txt(ctx,w-pad-4,toY(120)-5,'TP 1:2+','#26a69a',8,'right');
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'Silver Bullet: Sweep → MSS → FVG → Entry (вікно 1 година)','#1a1a1a',8);
};

// ── BREAKER BLOCK MODULE ──────────────────────────
window.drawBreakerBullish=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,215);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  // Price forms Bearish OB, breaks above it, OB flips to Bullish Breaker (support)
  const raw=[[112,108],[107,103],[102,107],[106,102],[101,106],[105,110],[109,114],[113,118],[117,122],[121,117],[116,113],[112,116],[115,120],[119,124]];
  const minP=99,maxP=128,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=pad;
  // Bearish OB zone (the failed one)
  zone(ctx,sx+1*step,toY(112),sx+4*step,toY(107),'#ef5350',0.08);
  txt(ctx,sx+2*step,toY(112)-6,'Bearish OB','#ef5350',7,'left');
  // Break level (where price closed above)
  hl(ctx,toY(112),sx+1*step,sx+8*step,'#fbbf24',[3,3]);txt(ctx,sx+6*step,toY(112)+11,'Pробій ↑','#fbbf24',7);
  // Bullish Breaker zone (flipped)
  zone(ctx,sx+8*step,toY(114),w-pad,toY(110),'#26a69a',0.15);
  txt(ctx,sx+9*step,toY(114)-6,'🔨 Bullish Breaker','#26a69a',8,'left');
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(Math.max(o,c)+1.5),toY(Math.min(o,c)-1),cw,c>=o));
  // Retest + entry
  arr(ctx,sx+11*step+cw/2,toY(114),sx+11*step+cw/2,toY(120),'#ec407a');
  txt(ctx,sx+11*step+cw+4,toY(117),'Entry','#ec407a',8,'left');
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'Bullish Breaker: failed Bearish OB = нова підтримка','#1a1a1a',8);
};

window.drawMarketOrder=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,190);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=14,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const prices=[100,102,104,101,103,106,104,107,110,108,112,109,113,111];
  const minP=97,maxP=117,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-prices.length*step*2)/2;
  // draw simple line + candles
  prices.forEach((p,i)=>{
    const o=p,c=p+(i%3-1)*1.5,hi=Math.max(o,c)+1.2,lo=Math.min(o,c)-0.8;
    cndl(ctx,sx+i*(step),toY(o),toY(c),toY(hi),toY(lo),cw,c>=o);
  });
  // Market order point - arrow straight into current price
  const entryX=sx+8*step+cw/2;
  const entryY=toY(prices[8]);
  // Flash circle
  ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.lineWidth=2;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(entryX,entryY,10,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.stroke();
  // Arrow
  arr(ctx,entryX,entryY-32,entryX,entryY-12,'#ef5350');
  txt(ctx,entryX+16,entryY-22,'Market Order','#ef5350',9,'left');
  txt(ctx,entryX+16,entryY-10,'Виконано миттєво','#fbbf24',8,'left');
  txt(ctx,entryX,entryY+18,'по ринковій ціні $'+prices[8],'#6b72a0',8);
  // Price label
  ctx.fillStyle='#ef5350';ctx.fillRect(w-58,entryY-8,56,16);
  ctx.fillStyle='#0a0b17';ctx.font=`bold 9px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='center';
  ctx.fillText('$'+prices[8],w-30,entryY+4);
};

window.drawLimitOrder=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const prices=[110,112,108,111,114,112,109,107,105,108,106,104,107,105];
  const minP=101,maxP=118,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-prices.length*step)/2;
  const limitPrice=104;
  const limitY=toY(limitPrice);
  // Limit line
  ctx.strokeStyle='#8b5cf6';ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.setLineDash([6,4]);
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(sx,limitY);ctx.lineTo(w-8,limitY);ctx.stroke();
  ctx.setLineDash([]);
  // Limit label
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(139,92,246,.15)';ctx.fillRect(w-70,limitY-9,68,18);
  ctx.fillStyle='#a78bfa';ctx.font=`bold 9px 'JetBrains Mono'`;ctx.textAlign='center';
  ctx.fillText('LIMIT $'+limitPrice,w-36,limitY+4);
  // Candles falling to limit
  prices.forEach((p,i)=>{
    const o=p,c=p-(i>8?1.2:0)+(i%2)*0.8,hi=Math.max(o,c)+1,lo=Math.min(o,c)-0.7;
    cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(hi),toY(lo),cw,c>=o);
  });
  // Touch point
  const touchX=sx+12*step+cw/2;
  ctx.strokeStyle='#26a69a';ctx.lineWidth=2;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(touchX,limitY,8,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,touchX,limitY-16,'✓ Виконано!','#26a69a',9);
  // Zone label
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(139,92,246,.06)';ctx.fillRect(sx,limitY,w-sx-8,h-limitY-4);
  txt(ctx,sx+30,limitY+18,'Ордер чекав тут','#6b72a0',8,'left');
};

window.drawStopOrder=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const prices=[100,102,105,103,106,108,106,109,112,110,113,111,108,106,103,100,98,96];
  const minP=93,maxP=117,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-prices.length*step)/2;
  const entryP=106,slP=99;
  // Entry zone
  hl(ctx,toY(entryP),sx,w-8,'#26a69a',[4,4]);
  txt(ctx,w-10,toY(entryP)-6,'Вхід $'+entryP,'#26a69a',8,'right');
  // Stop Loss line
  hl(ctx,toY(slP),sx,w-8,'#ef5350',[4,4]);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.1)';ctx.fillRect(sx,toY(slP),w-sx-8,h-toY(slP)-4);
  txt(ctx,w-10,toY(slP)-6,'Stop Loss $'+slP,'#ef5350',8,'right');
  // Candles
  prices.forEach((p,i)=>{
    const o=p,c=p+(i<10?1.2:-1.5)+(i%2)*0.6,hi=Math.max(o,c)+0.9,lo=Math.min(o,c)-0.7;
    cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(hi),toY(lo),cw,c>=o);
  });
  // Trigger point
  const trigX=sx+16*step+cw/2;
  ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.lineWidth=2;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(trigX,toY(slP),8,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,trigX,toY(slP)+18,'⚡ Стоп активовано','#ef5350',9);
};

  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;

             [103,108,111,101],[107,104,110,102],[103,106,109,100],[105,101,109,99],
             [100,98,102,95],[97,103,105,96],[102,108,111,101],[107,105,112,105]];
  const minP=92,maxP=116,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-raw.length*step)/2;
  const eqhY=toY(109.5),eqlY=toY(99.5);
  // EQH zone
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(251,191,36,.06)';ctx.fillRect(sx,eqhY-2,w-sx-8,14);
  hl(ctx,eqhY,sx,w-8,'#fbbf24',[5,3]);
