  txt(ctx,w-10,eqhY+12,'Стоп-лоси шортистів','#fbbf24',7,'right');
  // EQL zone
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(251,191,36,.06)';ctx.fillRect(sx,eqlY-2,w-sx-8,14);
  hl(ctx,eqlY,sx,w-8,'#fbbf24',[5,3]);
  txt(ctx,w-10,eqlY-8,'SSL / EQL','#fbbf24',8,'right');
  txt(ctx,w-10,eqlY+12,'Стоп-лоси лонгістів','#fbbf24',7,'right');
  // Draw candles
  raw.forEach(([o,c,hi,lo],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(hi),toY(lo),cw,c>=o));
  // Sweep arrow on last candles
  arr(ctx,sx+9*step+cw/2,toY(100),sx+9*step+cw/2,toY(95),'#ef5350');
  txt(ctx,sx+9*step+cw/2+2,toY(97)+12,'Sweep!','#ef5350',8,'left');
  arr(ctx,sx+10*step+cw/2,toY(97),sx+10*step+cw/2,toY(104),'#26a69a');
};

window.drawLiquidityCascade=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,195);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=18,cw=w-pad*2,ch=h-pad*2;
  // Cascade of stops visualization (horizontal bar chart)
  const levels=[
    {label:'$84,500 BSL',y:0.10,size:0.72,col:'#fbbf24',type:'bsl'},
    {label:'$83,200 BSL',y:0.22,size:0.55,col:'#fbbf24',type:'bsl'},
    {label:'► $82,800 Ціна',y:0.34,size:0,col:'#e8edf8',type:'price'},
    {label:'$82,100 SSL',y:0.52,size:0.48,col:'#ef5350',type:'ssl'},
    {label:'$81,500 SSL',y:0.64,size:0.62,col:'#ef5350',type:'ssl'},
    {label:'$80,800 SSL',y:0.76,size:0.80,col:'#ef5350',type:'ssl'},
  ];
  levels.forEach(l=>{
    const y=pad+l.y*ch;
    if(l.type==='price'){
      ctx.strokeStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.setLineDash([3,4]);
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(pad,y);ctx.lineTo(w-pad,y);ctx.stroke();
      ctx.setLineDash([]);
      txt(ctx,pad+4,y-4,l.label,'#e8edf8',9,'left');
      return;
    }
    const barW=l.size*(cw*0.5);
    const x=l.type==='bsl'?pad+(cw*0.5-barW):pad+(cw*0.5);
    ctx.fillStyle=l.col;ctx.globalAlpha=.15;ctx.fillRect(x,y-6,barW,12);ctx.globalAlpha=1;
    ctx.strokeStyle=l.col;ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.strokeRect(x,y-6,barW,12);
    txt(ctx,pad+4,y+4,l.label,l.col,8,'left');
    // Bar size label
    txt(ctx,x+barW+(l.type==='bsl'?4:-4),y+4,Math.round(l.size*100)+'% обʼєму',l.col,7,l.type==='bsl'?'left':'right');
  });
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-4,'Розподіл ліквідності відносно ціни','#6b72a0',8);
};

// ── CANDLESTICK ANATOMY DRAW FUNCTIONS ──────────────
window.drawCandleAnatomy=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,220);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cx=w/2,pad=20;
  // Bullish candle (left)
  const bx=cx-80,cw2=36,ch=120;
  const bOpen=h*0.65,bClose=h*0.22,bHigh=h*0.12,bLow=h*0.78;
  // Wick
  ctx.strokeStyle='#26a69a';ctx.lineWidth=2;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(bx+cw2/2,bHigh);ctx.lineTo(bx+cw2/2,bLow);ctx.stroke();
  // Body
  ctx.fillStyle='#26a69a';ctx.fillRect(bx,bClose,cw2,bOpen-bClose);
  // Labels
  const lx=bx-10;
  // High
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.2)';ctx.lineWidth=1;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(bx+cw2/2,bHigh);ctx.lineTo(lx-30,bHigh);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,lx-32,bHigh+4,'High','#fbbf24',9,'right');
  // Close
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(bx,bClose);ctx.lineTo(lx-30,bClose);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,lx-32,bClose+4,'Close','#26a69a',9,'right');
  // Open
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(bx,bOpen);ctx.lineTo(lx-30,bOpen);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,lx-32,bOpen+4,'Open','#26a69a',9,'right');
  // Low
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(bx+cw2/2,bLow);ctx.lineTo(lx-30,bLow);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,lx-32,bLow+4,'Low','#ef5350',9,'right');
  // Body brace
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(38,166,154,.4)';ctx.lineWidth=1;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(bx+cw2+4,bClose);ctx.lineTo(bx+cw2+10,bClose);
  ctx.lineTo(bx+cw2+10,(bClose+bOpen)/2);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,bx+cw2+14,(bClose+bOpen)/2+4,'Тіло','#26a69a',8,'left');

  // Bearish candle (right)
  const rx=cx+44;
  const rOpen=h*0.22,rClose=h*0.65,rHigh=h*0.12,rLow=h*0.78;
  ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.lineWidth=2;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(rx+cw2/2,rHigh);ctx.lineTo(rx+cw2/2,rLow);ctx.stroke();
  ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.3)';
  ctx.fillRect(rx,rOpen,cw2,rClose-rOpen);
  ctx.strokeRect(rx,rOpen,cw2,rClose-rOpen);

  // Right labels
  const rx2=rx+cw2+4;
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.2)';ctx.lineWidth=1;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(rx+cw2,rOpen);ctx.lineTo(rx2+28,rOpen);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,rx2+30,rOpen+4,'Open','#ef5350',9,'left');
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(rx+cw2,rClose);ctx.lineTo(rx2+28,rClose);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,rx2+30,rClose+4,'Close','#ef5350',9,'left');

  // Upper/lower wick labels
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.15)';
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(rx+cw2/2,rHigh);ctx.lineTo(rx2+28,rHigh);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,rx2+30,rHigh+4,'High','#fbbf24',9,'left');
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(rx+cw2/2,rLow);ctx.lineTo(rx2+28,rLow);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,rx2+30,rLow+4,'Low','#6b72a0',9,'left');

  // Title labels
  txt(ctx,bx+cw2/2,h-6,'🟢 Бичача','#26a69a',9);
  txt(ctx,rx+cw2/2,h-6,'🔴 Ведмежа','#ef5350',9);

  // Upper wick label for bullish
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.15)';ctx.lineWidth=1;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(bx+cw2/2,bHigh);ctx.lineTo(bx+cw2/2,bHigh-2);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,bx+cw2/2,bHigh-8,'Верхня тінь','#6b72a0',7);
  txt(ctx,bx+cw2/2,bLow+14,'Нижня тінь','#6b72a0',7);
};

window.drawCandleTypes=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const types=[
    {name:'Марибозу',sub:'Strong Bull',o:0.72,c:0.18,hi:0.16,lo:0.74,col:'#26a69a'},
    {name:'Доджі',sub:'Невизначеність',o:0.45,c:0.46,hi:0.15,lo:0.80,col:'#fbbf24'},
    {name:'Молот',sub:'Reversal Bull',o:0.40,c:0.35,hi:0.30,lo:0.88,col:'#26a69a'},
    {name:'Зірка',sub:'Reversal Bear',o:0.55,c:0.60,hi:0.18,lo:0.65,col:'#ef5350'},
    {name:'Поглинання',sub:'Strong Bear',o:0.20,c:0.75,hi:0.16,lo:0.78,col:'#ef5350'},
  ];
  const pad=20,cw=28,gap=(w-pad*2-types.length*cw)/(types.length-1),ch=h-pad*2-28;
  types.forEach((t,i)=>{
    const x=pad+i*(cw+gap);
    const open=pad+t.o*ch,close=pad+t.c*ch,high=pad+t.hi*ch,low=pad+t.lo*ch;
    // Wick
    ctx.strokeStyle=t.col;ctx.lineWidth=1.5;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x+cw/2,high);ctx.lineTo(x+cw/2,low);ctx.stroke();
    // Body
    const top=Math.min(open,close),bodyH=Math.max(2,Math.abs(open-close));
    if(t.col==='#26a69a'){ctx.fillStyle='#26a69a';ctx.fillRect(x+1,top,cw-2,bodyH);}
    else{ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.3)';ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.fillRect(x+1,top,cw-2,bodyH);ctx.strokeRect(x+1,top,cw-2,bodyH);}
    // Labels
    txt(ctx,x+cw/2,h-18,t.name,t.col,8);
    txt(ctx,x+cw/2,h-7,t.sub,'#6b72a0',7);
  });
};

window.drawCandlePatterns=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,215);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=16,cw=14,gap=4,step=cw+gap;
  // Left: Bullish engulfing setup
  const lx=pad;
  const lbleft=[
    {o:0.30,c:0.55,hi:0.25,lo:0.58,col:'#ef5350'},
    {o:0.50,c:0.58,hi:0.45,lo:0.62,col:'#ef5350'},
    {o:0.55,c:0.62,hi:0.52,lo:0.65,col:'#ef5350'},
    {o:0.60,c:0.58,hi:0.56,lo:0.72,col:'#ef5350'},   // small bear
    {o:0.68,c:0.28,hi:0.65,lo:0.72,col:'#26a69a'},   // big bull engulf
    {o:0.30,c:0.18,hi:0.27,lo:0.32,col:'#26a69a'},
    {o:0.20,c:0.12,hi:0.17,lo:0.22,col:'#26a69a'},
  ];
  const ch=h-pad*2-28;
  lbleft.forEach((t,i)=>{
    const x=lx+i*step;
    const open=pad+t.o*ch,close=pad+t.c*ch,high=pad+t.hi*ch,low=pad+t.lo*ch;
    ctx.strokeStyle=t.col;ctx.lineWidth=1.2;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x+cw/2,high);ctx.lineTo(x+cw/2,low);ctx.stroke();
    const top=Math.min(open,close),bh=Math.max(2,Math.abs(open-close));
    if(t.col==='#26a69a'){ctx.fillStyle='#26a69a';ctx.fillRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);}
    else{ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.28)';ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.fillRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);ctx.strokeRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);ctx.strokeStyle=t.col;}
  });
  // Bullish engulfing highlight
  const engX=lx+4*step;
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(38,166,154,.6)';ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.setLineDash([3,4]);
  ctx.strokeRect(engX-3,pad+0.24*ch,cw+6,0.52*ch);ctx.setLineDash([]);
  txt(ctx,engX+cw/2,pad+0.22*ch-6,'Bullish Engulfing','#26a69a',8);

  // Right: Rejection wick / hammer
  const rx=lx+8*step+20;
  const lbright=[
    {o:0.28,c:0.42,hi:0.24,lo:0.46,col:'#ef5350'},
    {o:0.40,c:0.50,hi:0.36,lo:0.54,col:'#ef5350'},
    {o:0.48,c:0.55,hi:0.42,lo:0.58,col:'#ef5350'},
    {o:0.53,c:0.45,hi:0.40,lo:0.82,col:'#26a69a'},  // hammer
    {o:0.45,c:0.30,hi:0.42,lo:0.48,col:'#26a69a'},
    {o:0.32,c:0.20,hi:0.28,lo:0.34,col:'#26a69a'},
  ];
  lbright.forEach((t,i)=>{
    const x=rx+i*step;
    const open=pad+t.o*ch,close=pad+t.c*ch,high=pad+t.hi*ch,low=pad+t.lo*ch;
    ctx.strokeStyle=t.col;ctx.lineWidth=1.2;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x+cw/2,high);ctx.lineTo(x+cw/2,low);ctx.stroke();
    const top=Math.min(open,close),bh=Math.max(2,Math.abs(open-close));
    if(t.col==='#26a69a'){ctx.fillStyle='#26a69a';ctx.fillRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);}
    else{ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.28)';ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.fillRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);ctx.strokeRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);ctx.strokeStyle=t.col;}
  });
  const hamX=rx+3*step;
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(38,166,154,.6)';ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.setLineDash([3,4]);
  ctx.strokeRect(hamX-3,pad+0.39*ch,cw+6,0.47*ch);ctx.setLineDash([]);
  txt(ctx,hamX+cw/2,pad+0.38*ch-6,'Молот / Hammer','#26a69a',8);

  // Divider
  hl(ctx,h/2,lx+8*step,lx+8*step,'#1e2040',[]);
  ctx.strokeStyle='#1e2040';ctx.lineWidth=1;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(lx+8*step+8,pad);ctx.lineTo(lx+8*step+8,h-8);ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-6,'Ключові свічкові патерни розвороту','#6b72a0',8);
};

window.drawTimeframes=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const tfs=['1W','1D','4H','1H','15M'];
  const cols=['#fbbf24','#fb923c','#8b5cf6','#5b9fff','#26a69a'];
  const candleNums=[4,7,12,18,26];
  const pad=14,ch=h-pad*2;
  const colW=(w-pad*2)/tfs.length;
  tfs.forEach((tf,ti)=>{
    const bx=pad+ti*colW+4;
    const bw=colW-8;
    const n=candleNums[ti];
    const cw=Math.floor(bw/n)-1;
    const step=cw+1;
    const sx=bx+(bw-n*step)/2;
    // Generate mini candles
    let p=0.5;
    const bias=ti<2?0.55:ti===2?0.50:ti===3?0.48:0.52;
    for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
      const r=Math.sin(ti*100+i*17.3)*0.5+0.5;
      const bull=r<bias;
      const body=0.04+r*0.08;
      const o=p,c=bull?Math.min(0.9,o+body):Math.max(0.1,o-body);
      const wi=body*0.5,wk=body*0.4;
      const cy1=pad+Math.min(o,c)*ch,cy2=pad+Math.max(o,c)*ch;
      const hi=pad+(Math.min(o,c)-wi)*ch,lo=pad+(Math.max(o,c)+wk)*ch;
      ctx.strokeStyle=cols[ti];ctx.lineWidth=1;
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(sx+i*step+cw/2,hi);ctx.lineTo(sx+i*step+cw/2,lo);ctx.stroke();
      if(bull){ctx.fillStyle=cols[ti];ctx.fillRect(sx+i*step,cy1,Math.max(1,cw-1),Math.max(1,cy2-cy1));}
      else{ctx.strokeStyle=cols[ti];ctx.strokeRect(sx+i*step,cy1,Math.max(1,cw-1),Math.max(1,cy2-cy1));ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.2)';ctx.fillRect(sx+i*step,cy1,Math.max(1,cw-1),Math.max(1,cy2-cy1));}
      p=c;
    }
    // TF label
    ctx.fillStyle=cols[ti];ctx.font=`bold 12px 'Bebas Neue'`;ctx.textAlign='center';
    ctx.fillText(tf,bx+bw/2,h-4);
    // Divider
    if(ti<tfs.length-1){ctx.strokeStyle='#121325';ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(bx+bw+4,pad);ctx.lineTo(bx+bw+4,h-20);ctx.stroke();}
  });
};

window.drawReadingCandles=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,210);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=15,gap=5,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  // A story: downtrend → reversal → uptrend
  const story=[
    {o:0.20,c:0.38,hi:0.16,lo:0.42,col:'#ef5350',note:''},
    {o:0.36,c:0.50,hi:0.33,lo:0.54,col:'#ef5350',note:''},
    {o:0.48,c:0.60,hi:0.44,lo:0.64,col:'#ef5350',note:''},
    {o:0.58,c:0.45,hi:0.40,lo:0.82,col:'#26a69a',note:'🔨'},  // hammer
    {o:0.47,c:0.35,hi:0.44,lo:0.40,col:'#26a69a',note:''},
    {o:0.37,c:0.26,hi:0.33,lo:0.28,col:'#26a69a',note:''},
    {o:0.27,c:0.18,hi:0.24,lo:0.20,col:'#26a69a',note:''},
    {o:0.19,c:0.28,hi:0.16,lo:0.30,col:'#26a69a',note:''},
    {o:0.27,c:0.18,hi:0.24,lo:0.30,col:'#ef5350',note:''},  // doji area
    {o:0.20,c:0.19,hi:0.12,lo:0.24,col:'#fbbf24',note:'⚡'},  // doji
    {o:0.21,c:0.10,hi:0.18,lo:0.12,col:'#26a69a',note:''},
    {o:0.11,c:0.04,hi:0.09,lo:0.06,col:'#26a69a',note:''},
    {o:0.05,c:0.12,hi:0.04,lo:0.14,col:'#26a69a',note:''},
  ];
  const ch=h-pad*2-22;
  const sx=(w-story.length*step)/2;
  story.forEach((t,i)=>{
    const x=sx+i*step;
    const open=pad+t.o*ch,close=pad+t.c*ch,high=pad+t.hi*ch,low=pad+t.lo*ch;
    ctx.strokeStyle=t.col;ctx.lineWidth=1.2;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x+cw/2,high);ctx.lineTo(x+cw/2,low);ctx.stroke();
    const top=Math.min(open,close),bh=Math.max(2,Math.abs(open-close));
    if(t.col==='#26a69a'){ctx.fillStyle='#26a69a';ctx.fillRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);}
    else if(t.col==='#fbbf24'){
      ctx.strokeStyle='#fbbf24';ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.strokeRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,Math.max(2,bh));
    }
    else{ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.28)';ctx.strokeStyle='#ef5350';ctx.fillRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);ctx.strokeRect(x+.5,top,cw-1,bh);}
    if(t.note){txt(ctx,x+cw/2,high-10,t.note,t.col==='#fbbf24'?'#fbbf24':'#26a69a',12);}
  });
  // Annotations
  txt(ctx,sx+1*step,h-6,'↓ Падіння','#ef5350',8,'left');
  txt(ctx,sx+8*step,h-6,'⚡ Доджі','#fbbf24',8);
  txt(ctx,sx+11*step,h-6,'↑ Зростання','#26a69a',8,'left');
  // Arrow phases
  arr(ctx,sx,pad+ch*0.4,sx+4*step,pad+ch*0.6,'rgba(239,83,80,.3)');
  arr(ctx,sx+9*step,pad+ch*0.22,sx+13*step,pad+ch*0.04,'rgba(38,166,154,.3)');
};

// ── NEW DRAW FUNCTIONS ──────────────────────────────
window.drawIPDA=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,220);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[100,108],[107,116],[115,124],[123,115],[114,122],[121,130],[129,118],[117,108],[107,115],[114,122],[121,131],[130,122],[121,130],[129,140]];
  const minP=100,maxP=145,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-raw.length*step)/2;
  // External structure range
  const extY1=toY(108),extY2=toY(131);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(251,191,36,.04)';ctx.fillRect(sx,extY2,w-sx*2,extY1-extY2);
  hl(ctx,extY1,sx,w-6,'#fbbf24',[6,4]);hl(ctx,extY2,sx,w-6,'#fbbf24',[6,4]);
  txt(ctx,w-10,extY1+12,'External','#fbbf24',8,'right');txt(ctx,w-10,extY2-5,'External','#fbbf24',8,'right');
  // Internal BOS
  hl(ctx,toY(122),sx+6*step,sx+10*step,'#8b5cf6',[3,4]);
  txt(ctx,sx+8*step+cw/2,toY(122)-6,'Internal BOS','#8b5cf6',8);
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>{
    const hi=Math.max(o,c)+2.5,lo=Math.min(o,c)-2;
    cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(hi),toY(lo),cw,c>=o);
  });
  txt(ctx,sx+cw/2,h-6,'IPDA: External structure визначає напрямок','#6b72a0',8,'left');
};

window.drawIDM=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,220);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[100,108],[107,115],[114,106],[105,112],[111,103],[102,112],[111,120],[119,128],[127,119],[118,126],[125,134],[133,125],[124,132],[131,141]];
  const minP=98,maxP=146,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-raw.length*step)/2;
  // IDM level
  const idmY=toY(115);
  hl(ctx,idmY,sx+2*step,sx+8*step,'#ef5350',[4,4]);
  txt(ctx,sx+2*step+4,idmY-6,'IDM (пастка)','#ef5350',8,'left');
  // Real OB zone
  zone(ctx,sx+4*step,toY(106),w-6,toY(102),'#5b9fff',0.12);
  txt(ctx,sx+4*step+4,toY(106)-6,'Справжній OB','#5b9fff',8,'left');
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>{
    const hi=Math.max(o,c)+2,lo=Math.min(o,c)-1.5;
    cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(hi),toY(lo),cw,c>=o);
  });
  arr(ctx,sx+4*step+cw/2,toY(103),sx+4*step+cw/2,toY(120),'#26a69a');
  txt(ctx,sx+5*step,toY(112)+14,'Реальний рух↑','#26a69a',8,'left');
  txt(ctx,sx+6*step+cw/2,h-5,'❌ Новачок входить тут → Sweep → ✅ Вхід після OB','#6b72a0',8);
};

window.drawMitigation=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,220);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=14,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[130,138],[137,132],[131,122],[121,112],[111,120],[119,128],[127,138],[137,130],[129,122],[121,115],[114,120],[119,128],[127,120],[119,112]];
  const minP=108,maxP=145,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-raw.length*step)/2;
  // Bearish OB zone (unmitigated)
  zone(ctx,sx+1*step,toY(138),sx+4*step+cw,toY(130),'#ef5350',0.12);
  txt(ctx,sx+1*step+4,toY(138)-6,'Bearish OB','#ef5350',8,'left');
  // Mitigation arrow
  arr(ctx,sx+7*step+cw/2,toY(127),sx+2*step+cw/2,toY(133),'#fbbf24');
  txt(ctx,sx+4*step+cw/2,toY(130)-10,'Мітигація','#fbbf24',8);
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>{
    const hi=Math.max(o,c)+2,lo=Math.min(o,c)-1.5;
    cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(hi),toY(lo),cw,c>=o);
  });
  txt(ctx,sx+2*step+cw/2,toY(122)-8,'↓ Банк закриває збиткові ордери','#fbbf24',8);
};

window.drawUnmitigated=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,210);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[100,108],[107,116],[115,106],[105,115],[114,124],[123,115],[114,104],[103,113],[112,122],[121,131],[130,122],[121,130]];
  const minP=98,maxP=137,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-raw.length*step)/2;
  // OB1 — mitigated (grey)
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(107,114,160,.08)';ctx.strokeStyle='#6b72a0';ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.setLineDash([3,4]);
  ctx.fillRect(sx+2*step,toY(115),3*step,toY(105)-toY(115));
  ctx.strokeRect(sx+2*step,toY(115),3*step,toY(105)-toY(115));ctx.setLineDash([]);
  txt(ctx,sx+3*step+cw/2,toY(115)-5,'✓ Мітигований','#6b72a0',8);
  // OB2 — unmitigated (blue)
  zone(ctx,sx+6*step,toY(115),w-6,toY(103),'#5b9fff',0.12);
  txt(ctx,sx+6*step+4,toY(115)-6,'⬛ Немітигований OB','#5b9fff',8,'left');
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>{
    cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(Math.max(o,c)+2),toY(Math.min(o,c)-1.5),cw,c>=o);
  });
};

window.drawPremDisc=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=20,cw=w-pad*2,ch=h-pad*2;
  // Swing range
  const swingLo=0.7,swingHi=0.15;
  const yLo=pad+swingLo*ch,yHi=pad+swingHi*ch,yMid=(yLo+yHi)/2;
  // Premium zone (red)
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.07)';ctx.fillRect(pad,yHi,cw,yMid-yHi);
  // Discount zone (green)
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(38,166,154,.07)';ctx.fillRect(pad,yMid,cw,yLo-yMid);
  hl(ctx,yHi,pad,pad+cw,'#ef5350',[4,4]);hl(ctx,yLo,pad,pad+cw,'#26a69a',[4,4]);
  hl(ctx,yMid,pad,pad+cw,'#fbbf24',[2,5]);
  txt(ctx,w-12,yHi+12,'🔴 Premium','#ef5350',9,'right');
  txt(ctx,w-12,yMid-5,'Equilibrium 50%','#fbbf24',9,'right');
  txt(ctx,w-12,yLo-5,'🟢 Discount','#26a69a',9,'right');
  // OB in discount
  zone(ctx,pad+30,yLo-35,pad+cw-20,yLo-18,'#5b9fff',0.15);
  txt(ctx,pad+35,yLo-38,'Bullish OB (Discount)','#5b9fff',8,'left');
  // Arrow up
  arr(ctx,pad+cw/2,yLo-15,pad+cw/2,yHi+20,'#26a69a');
  txt(ctx,pad+cw/2+10,yMid,'Рух у Premium','#26a69a',8,'left');
};

window.drawWyckoffAcc=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,230);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=20,cw=w-pad*2,ch=h-60;
  const phases=[
    {name:'A',col:'rgba(91,159,255,.12)',border:'#5b9fff',x:0,ww:.18},
    {name:'B',col:'rgba(139,92,246,.1)',border:'#8b5cf6',x:.19,ww:.30},
    {name:'C',col:'rgba(239,83,80,.1)',border:'#ef5350',x:.50,ww:.12},
    {name:'D',col:'rgba(38,166,154,.1)',border:'#26a69a',x:.63,ww:.20},
    {name:'E',col:'rgba(251,191,36,.1)',border:'#fbbf24',x:.84,ww:.16},
  ];
  phases.forEach(ph=>{
    const px=pad+ph.x*cw,pw=ph.ww*cw;
    ctx.fillStyle=ph.col;ctx.fillRect(px,pad,pw,ch);
    ctx.strokeStyle=ph.border;ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.strokeRect(px,pad,pw,ch);
    txt(ctx,px+pw/2,h-32,ph.name,ph.border,14);
  });
  // Price path for accumulation
  const pts=[[0,.55],[.08,.58],[.12,.48],[.17,.52],[.22,.50],[.30,.53],[.38,.49],[.45,.55],[.50,.60],[.52,.65],[.56,.50],[.62,.53],[.68,.45],[.73,.42],[.78,.38],[.84,.35],[.88,.28],[.94,.22],[1,.18]];
  ctx.strokeStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.lineWidth=1.8;ctx.beginPath();
  pts.forEach(([px,py],i)=>{const x=pad+px*cw,y=pad+py*ch;i===0?ctx.moveTo(x,y):ctx.lineTo(x,y);});
  ctx.stroke();
  // Spring label
  const sx=pad+.51*cw,sy=pad+.65*ch;
  ctx.fillStyle='#ef5350';ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(sx,sy,4,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();
  txt(ctx,sx,sy+14,'Spring','#ef5350',8);
  // Labels
  const wLabels=[['SC',.10,.50],['AR',.14,.46],['ST',.35,.52],['SOS',.76,.38],['LPS',.82,.35]];
  wLabels.forEach(([l,px,py])=>{
    txt(ctx,pad+px*cw,pad+py*ch-8,l,'#6b72a0',7);
  });
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-8,'Wyckoff Accumulation Schematic','#6b72a0',8);
};

window.drawWyckoffDist=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,230);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=20,cw=w-pad*2,ch=h-60;
  const phases=[
    {name:'A',col:'rgba(91,159,255,.1)',border:'#5b9fff',x:0,ww:.18},
    {name:'B',col:'rgba(139,92,246,.1)',border:'#8b5cf6',x:.19,ww:.28},
    {name:'C',col:'rgba(251,146,60,.12)',border:'#fb923c',x:.48,ww:.12},
    {name:'D',col:'rgba(239,83,80,.1)',border:'#ef5350',x:.61,ww:.22},
    {name:'E',col:'rgba(251,191,36,.08)',border:'#fbbf24',x:.84,ww:.16},
  ];
  phases.forEach(ph=>{
    const px=pad+ph.x*cw,pw=ph.ww*cw;
    ctx.fillStyle=ph.col;ctx.fillRect(px,pad,pw,ch);
    ctx.strokeStyle=ph.border;ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.strokeRect(px,pad,pw,ch);
    txt(ctx,px+pw/2,h-32,ph.name,ph.border,14);
  });
  const pts=[[0,.55],[.08,.50],[.12,.60],[.17,.52],[.25,.48],[.33,.54],[.40,.48],[.48,.40],[.52,.35],[.56,.48],[.62,.42],[.68,.52],[.73,.58],[.78,.62],[.84,.60],[.90,.68],[.95,.74],[1,.80]];
  ctx.strokeStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.lineWidth=1.8;ctx.beginPath();
  pts.forEach(([px,py],i)=>{const x=pad+px*cw,y=pad+py*ch;i===0?ctx.moveTo(x,y):ctx.lineTo(x,y);});
  ctx.stroke();
  // Upthrust
  const utx=pad+.51*cw,uty=pad+.35*ch;
  ctx.fillStyle='#ef5350';ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(utx,uty,4,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();
  txt(ctx,utx,uty-8,'UT','#ef5350',8);
  txt(ctx,w/2,h-8,'Wyckoff Distribution Schematic','#6b72a0',8);
};

window.drawRetailVsSmart=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,220);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=13,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[100,108],[107,116],[115,124],[123,118],[117,108],[107,116],[115,110],[109,105],[104,115],[114,124],[123,134],[133,125],[124,132]];
  const minP=98,maxP=140,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-raw.length*step)/2;
  // Support level
  hl(ctx,toY(108),sx,w-6,'rgba(91,159,255,.4)',[5,4]);
  // Retail entry (wrong)
  txt(ctx,sx+1*step+cw/2,toY(108)-10,'❌ Retail буй','#ef5350',8);
  // Stop hunt zone
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(239,83,80,.07)';ctx.fillRect(sx+6*step,toY(108),3*step+cw,toY(104)-toY(108));
  txt(ctx,sx+7*step+cw/2,toY(106)+14,'Stop Hunt','#ef5350',8);
  // Smart entry (after sweep)
  zone(ctx,sx+8*step,toY(107),sx+11*step,toY(103),'#5b9fff',0.1);
  txt(ctx,sx+8*step+4,toY(104)-6,'✅ Smart вхід','#26a69a',8,'left');
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(Math.max(o,c)+2),toY(Math.min(o,c)-1.5),cw,c>=o));
};

window.drawIPDAMap=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,190);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const pad=18;
  // Three levels horizontal
  const levels=[
    {y:0.15,label:'Weekly BSL (HTF Ціль)',col:'#fbbf24',dash:[6,4]},
    {y:0.50,label:'4H OB Zone (Зона входу)',col:'#5b9fff',dash:[4,4]},
    {y:0.72,label:'Поточна ціна',col:'#e8edf8',dash:[]},
    {y:0.88,label:'Weekly SSL (IDM)',col:'#ef5350',dash:[5,4]},
  ];
  levels.forEach(l=>{
    const y=pad+l.y*(h-pad*2);
    ctx.strokeStyle=l.col;ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.setLineDash(l.dash);
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(pad,y);ctx.lineTo(w-pad,y);ctx.stroke();
    ctx.setLineDash([]);
    txt(ctx,pad+4,y-4,l.label,l.col,8,'left');
  });
  // Current price dot
  const curY=pad+0.72*(h-pad*2);
  ctx.fillStyle='#e8edf8';ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(w/2,curY,5,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fill();
  // Arrow up to target
  arr(ctx,w/2,curY-8,w/2,pad+0.18*(h-pad*2),'rgba(38,166,154,.5)');
  txt(ctx,w/2+12,pad+0.4*(h-pad*2),'IPDA доставить ціну','rgba(38,166,154,.6)',8,'left');
};

window.drawHighRR=function(canvas){
  const{ctx,w,h}=setupC(canvas,200);tvBg(ctx,w,h);
  const cw=12,gap=4,step=cw+gap,pad=22;
  const raw=[[100,108],[107,116],[115,106],[105,100],[99,108],[107,116],[115,124],[123,132],[131,141],[140,132],[131,140],[139,148],[147,156]];
  const minP=95,maxP=165,range=maxP-minP;
  const toY=p=>pad+(1-(p-minP)/range)*(h-pad*2);
  const sx=(w-raw.length*step)/2;
  // SL line (tight)
  hl(ctx,toY(97),sx+4*step,sx+8*step,'#ef5350',[3,4]);
  txt(ctx,sx+4*step+4,toY(97)+12,'SL',    '#ef5350',8,'left');
  // Entry
  hl(ctx,toY(100),sx+4*step,sx+8*step,'#8b5cf6',[3,4]);
  txt(ctx,sx+4*step+4,toY(100)-5,'Entry','#8b5cf6',8,'left');
  // TP
  hl(ctx,toY(156),sx+4*step,w-6,'#fbbf24',[4,4]);
  txt(ctx,w-10,toY(156)-5,'HTF BSL (TP)','#fbbf24',8,'right');
  // RR label
  const rrH=toY(97)-toY(156);
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(139,92,246,.3)';ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(sx+3*step,toY(100));ctx.lineTo(sx+2*step,toY(100));ctx.lineTo(sx+2*step,toY(156));ctx.lineTo(sx+3*step,toY(156));ctx.stroke();
  txt(ctx,sx+1*step,toY(100)+(toY(156)-toY(100))/2+4,'1:10+','#8b5cf6',10);
  raw.forEach(([o,c],i)=>cndl(ctx,sx+i*step,toY(o),toY(c),toY(Math.max(o,c)+2),toY(Math.min(o,c)-1.5),cw,c>=o));
};

function renderGloss(){
  document.getElementById('glossList').innerHTML=GLOSS.map((g,i)=>`
    <div class="gi" onclick="toggleG(${i})">
      <div class="gi-top">
        <div class="gi-term">${g.t}</div>
        <div class="gi-right">
          <div class="gi-tag" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.05);color:${g.tc}">${g.tag}</div>
          <div class="gi-chev" id="gc${i}">▾</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="gi-def" id="gd${i}">${g.d}</div>
    </div>`).join('');
}
function toggleG(i){document.getElementById('gd'+i).classList.toggle('open');document.getElementById('gc'+i).classList.toggle('open');}

// ═══════════ AUTH / PROFILE ═══════════
function initials(name){
  if(!name) return '?';
  const parts = name.trim().split(/\s+/);
  return (parts[0][0] + (parts[1]?parts[1][0]:'')).toUpperCase();
}

function setAvatar(el, user){
  if (!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = '';
  if (user && user.photo_url) {
    const img = document.createElement('img');
    img.src = user.photo_url;
    img.alt = '';
    img.onerror = () => { el.textContent = initials(user.first_name || user.username || '?'); };
    el.appendChild(img);
  } else {
    el.textContent = initials((user && (user.first_name || user.username)) || 'S');
  }
}

function fullName(u){
  if (!u) return 'Гість';
  return [u.first_name, u.last_name].filter(Boolean).join(' ') || u.username || 'Користувач';
}

function renderAuthCard(){
  const card = document.getElementById('auth-card');
  const nameEl = document.getElementById('auth-name');
  const unameEl = document.getElementById('auth-uname');
  const badgeEl = document.getElementById('auth-badge');
  const statusEl = document.getElementById('auth-status');
  const btn = document.getElementById('btn-start');

  if (!card) return;
  card.style.display = 'flex';
  setAvatar(document.getElementById('auth-avatar'), USER);
  nameEl.textContent = fullName(USER);
  unameEl.textContent = USER && USER.username ? '@' + USER.username : 'ID ' + (USER && USER.id ? USER.id : '—');

  if (USE_CLOUD) {
    badgeEl.textContent = 'TG';
    badgeEl.className = 'auth-badge tg';
    statusEl.className = 'auth-status ok';
    statusEl.innerHTML = '<span class="dot"></span>Підключено · CloudStorage активний';
  } else {
    badgeEl.textContent = 'GUEST';
    badgeEl.className = 'auth-badge guest';
    statusEl.className = 'auth-status';
    statusEl.innerHTML = '<span class="dot" style="background:var(--liq)"></span>Гостьовий режим · локальне збереження';
  }

  // Button label: new vs returning user
  if (ls('smc_registered', false)) {
    btn.textContent = 'Продовжити →';
  } else {
    btn.textContent = 'Зареєструватися та почати →';
  }
}

function registerAndStart(){
  if (!ls('smc_registered', false)) {
    lsSave('smc_registered', true);
    lsSave('smc_registered_at', Date.now());
    // Also persist a copy of the Telegram profile for display (cloud-synced)
    if (USER) {
      lsSave('smc_profile', {
        id: USER.id,
        first_name: USER.first_name,
        last_name: USER.last_name,
        username: USER.username,
        photo_url: USER.photo_url,
        lang: USER.language_code
      });
    }
    showToast('✅ Акаунт зареєстровано');
  }
  goHome();
}

function renderHeaderProfile(){
  setAvatar(document.getElementById('hdr-avatar'), USER);
  document.getElementById('hdr-user-name').textContent = fullName(USER);
  document.getElementById('hdr-user-sub').textContent = USER && USER.username ? '@' + USER.username : (USE_CLOUD ? 'Telegram' : 'Guest');
  const greet = document.getElementById('home-greeting');
  if (greet && USER && USER.first_name) {
    greet.textContent = 'Привіт, ' + USER.first_name + '! Обери шлях навчання';
  }
}

function openProfile(){
  updateProfileSheet();
  document.getElementById('profile-sheet').classList.add('open');
}
function closeProfile(){
  document.getElementById('profile-sheet').classList.remove('open');
}
function updateProfileSheet(){
  setAvatar(document.getElementById('prof-avatar'), USER);
  document.getElementById('prof-name').textContent = fullName(USER);
  document.getElementById('prof-uname').textContent = USER && USER.username ? '@' + USER.username : '—';
  document.getElementById('prof-id').textContent = USER && USER.id ? USER.id : '—';
  document.getElementById('prof-pts').textContent = getPoints();
  const doneCount = (ls('smc_done', []) || []).length;
  document.getElementById('prof-mods').textContent = doneCount;
  // Progress % — rough: modules out of 22 total
  const pct = Math.min(100, Math.round(doneCount / 22 * 100));
  document.getElementById('prof-prog').textContent = pct + '%';
  document.getElementById('prof-sim').textContent = ls('smc_sim_best', 0);

  const dot = document.getElementById('prof-sync-dot');
  const badge = document.getElementById('prof-sync-badge');
  if (USE_CLOUD && SYNC_STATUS === 'ok') {
    dot.className = 'sync-dot';
    badge.textContent = 'Telegram Cloud ✓';
  } else if (USE_CLOUD) {
    dot.className = 'sync-dot off';
    badge.textContent = 'Cloud · перевіряється';
  } else {
    dot.className = 'sync-dot off';
    badge.textContent = 'Локально (гість)';
  }
}

// ═══════════ INIT ═══════════
async function bootstrap(){
  const splashText = document.getElementById('splash-text');

  // 1. Detect Telegram WebApp
  if (TG) {
    try {
      TG.ready();
      TG.expand();
      // Apply Telegram theme colors if exposed (optional nicety)
      if (TG.setHeaderColor) { try { TG.setHeaderColor('#07080f'); } catch {} }
      if (TG.setBackgroundColor) { try { TG.setBackgroundColor('#07080f'); } catch {} }
    } catch {}
    USER = (TG.initDataUnsafe && TG.initDataUnsafe.user) || null;
    USE_CLOUD = !!(TG.CloudStorage && TG.CloudStorage.getItems);
  }

  // 2. Guest fallback (browser preview / dev)
  if (!USER) {
    USER = { id: 'guest', first_name: 'Гість', username: null, photo_url: null };
  }

  splashText.textContent = USE_CLOUD ? 'Завантаження з Telegram Cloud…' : 'Завантаження локально…';

  // 3. Load all progress data into in-memory cache
  await loadUserData();

  // 4. Hydrate existing runtime state that was read at module top
  done = new Set(ls('smc_done', []));
  quizDone = new Set(ls('smc_quiz_done', []));

  // 5. Render UI now that data is available
  renderAuthCard();
  renderHeaderProfile();
  updPtsDisplay();
  setRisk(1);

  // 6. Hide splash
  const splash = document.getElementById('splash');
  splash.style.opacity = '0';
  splash.style.transition = 'opacity .3s';
  setTimeout(() => splash.style.display = 'none', 320);
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => { bootstrap(); });
</script>
</body>
</html>
